athottarabhāgaprāramabhaḥ
śrutvā pādaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu krāntaṃ sūtena dhīmatā 
tataścaturthaṃ papracchuḥ pādaṃ vai ṛṣisattamāḥ  BndP 
pādaḥ krāntastṛtīyo 'yamanuṣaṅgeṇa nastvayā 
caturthaṃ vistarātpādaṃ saṃhāraṃ pārikīrttaya  BndP 
manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi pūrvāṇyevāparaiḥ saha 
saptarṣīṇāmathaiteṣāṃ sāṃpratasyāntare manoḥ  BndP 
vistarāvayavaṃ caiva nisargasya mahātmanaḥ 
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca sarvameva bravīhi naḥ  BndP 
sūta uvāca
bhavatāṃ kathayiṣyāmi sarvametadyathātatham 
pādaṃ tvimaṃ sasaṃhāraṃ caturthaṃ munisattamāḥ  BndP 
manorvaivasvatasyemaṃ sāṃpratasya mahātmaṃnaḥ 
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca nisargaṃ śṛṇuta dvijāḥ  BndP 
manvantarāṇāṃ saṃkṣepaṃ bhaviṣyaiḥ saha saptabhiḥ 
pralayaṃ caiva lokānāṃ bruvato me nibodhata  BndP 
etānyuktāni vai samyaksaptasaptasu vai prajāḥ 
manvantarāṇi saṃkṣepācchṛṇutā nāgatāni me  BndP 
sāvarṇasya pravakṣyāmi manorvaivasvatasya ha 
bhaviṣyasya bhaviṣyaṃ tu samāsāttannibodhata  BndP 
anāgatāśca saptaiva smṛtāstviha maharṣayaḥ 
kauśiko gālavaścaiva jāmadagnyaśca bhārgavaḥ  BndP 
dvaipāyano vaśiṣṭaśca kṛpaḥ śāradvatastathā 
ātreyo dīptimāṃścaiva ṛṣayaśṛṅgastu kāśyapaḥ  BndP 
bharadvājastathā drauṇiraśvatthāmā mahāyaśāḥ 
ete sapta mahātmāno bhaviṣyāḥ paramarṣayaḥ 
sutapāścāmitābhāśca sukhāścaiva gaṇāstrayaḥ  BndP 
teṣāṃ gaṇastu devānāmekaiko viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
nāmatastu pravakṣyāmi nibodhadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ  BndP 
ṛtustapaśca śukraśca kṛtirnemiḥ prabhākaraḥ 
prabhāso māsakṛddharmastejoraśmiḥ kraturvirāṭ  BndP 
arciṣmān dyotano bhānuryaśaḥ kīrttirbudho dhṛtiḥ  BndP 
viṃśatiḥ sutapā hyete nāmabhiḥ parikīrttitāḥ 
prabhurvibhurvibhāsaśca jetā hantā rihā ṛtuḥ  BndP 
sumatiḥ pramatirdīptiḥ samākhyāto maho mahān 
dehī munirinaḥ poṣṭā samaḥ satyaśca viśrutaḥ  BndP 
ityetehyamitābhāstu viṃśatiḥ parikīrttitāḥ 
dāmo dānī ṛtaḥ somo vittaṃ vaidyo yamo nidhiḥ  BndP 
homo havyaṃ hutaṃ dānaṃ deyaṃ dātā tapaḥ śamaḥ 
dhruvaṃ sthānaṃ vidhānaṃ ca niyamaśceti viṃśatiḥ  BndP 
sukhā hyete samākhyātāḥ sāvarṇye pratharmetare 
mārīcasyaiva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP 
sāṃpratasya bhaviṣyanti ṣaṣṭirdevāstadantare 
sāvarṇasya manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti navaiva tu  BndP 
virajāścārvarīvāṃśca nirmokādyāstathā pare 
nava cānyeṣu vakṣyāmi sāvarṇeṣvantareṣu vai  BndP 
sāvarṇamanavaścānye bhaviṣyā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ 
merusāvarṇitaste vai catvāro divyadṛṣṭayaḥ  BndP 
dakṣasya te hi vauhitrāḥ kriyāyā duhituḥ sutāḥ 
mahatā tapasā yuktā merupṛṣṭhe mahau jasaḥ  BndP 
brahmādibhistejanitā dakṣeṇaiva ca dhīmatā 
maharlokaṃ gatā vṛttā bhaviṣyā merumāśritāḥ  BndP 
mahānubhāvāste pūrvaṃ jajñire cākṣuṣentare 
jajñire manavaste hi bhaviṣyānāgatāntare  BndP 
prācetasasya dakṣasya dauhitrā manavastu ye 
sāvarṇā nāmataḥ pañca catvāraḥ paramarṣijāḥ  BndP 
saṃjñāputrastu sāvarṇireko vaivasvatastathā 
jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃjñāsuto nāma murvaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ  BndP 
vaivasvateṃ'tare prāpte samutpattistayoḥ śubhā 
caturdaśaite manavaḥ kīrtitā kīrtivarddhanāḥ  BndP 
vede smṛtau purāṇe ca sarve te prabhaviṣṇavaḥ 
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve bhūtānāṃ patayaḥ sthitāḥ  BndP 
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā 
pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ vai paripālyā nareśvaraiḥ  BndP 
prajābhistapasā caiva vistarasteṣu vakṣyate 
caturddaśaite vijñeyāḥ sargāḥ svāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ  BndP 
manvantarādhikāreṣu varttante 'tra sakṛtsakṛt 
vinivṛttādhikārāste mahārlokaṃ samāśritāḥ  BndP 
samatītāstu ye teṣāmaṣṭau ṣaṭ ca tathāpare 
pūrveṣu sāṃprataścāyaṃ śāsti vaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ  BndP 
ye śiṣṭāstānpravakṣyāmi saha devarṣidānavaiḥ 
saha prajā nisargeṇa sarvāṃste 'nāgatāndvijaḥ  BndP 
vaivasvata nisargeṇa teṣāṃ jñeyastu vistaraḥ 
anūnā nātiriktāste yasmātmarve vivasvataḥ  BndP 
punaruktabahutvāttu na vakṣye teṣu vistaram 
manvantareṣu bhāvyeṣu bhūteṣvapi tathaiva ca  BndP 
kulekule nisargāstu tasmājjñeyā vibhāgaśaḥ 
teṣāmeva hi siddhyarthaṃ vistareṇa krameṇa ca  BndP 
dakṣasya kanyā dharmiṣṭhā suvratā nāma viśrutā 
sarvakanyāvariṣṭhā tu jyeṣṭhā yā vīriṇīsutā  BndP 
gṛhītvā tāṃ pitā kanyāṃ jagāma brahmaṇo 'tike 
vairājasthamupāsīnaṃ dharmeṇa ca bhavena ca  BndP 
bhavadharmasamīpasthaṃ dakṣaṃ brahmābhyabhāṣata 
dakṣa kanyā taveyaṃ vai janayiṣyati suvratā  BndP 
caturo vai manūnputrāṃścāturvarṇyakarāñchubhān 
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo dharmo bhavastadā  BndP 
tāṃ kanyāṃ manasā jagmustrayaste brahmaṇā saha 
satyābhidhyāyināṃ teṣāṃ sadyaḥ kanyā vyajāyata  BndP 
sadṛśānūpatasteṣāṃ caturo vai kumārakān 
saṃsiddhāḥ kāryakaraṇe saṃbhūtāste śriyānvitāḥ  BndP 
upabhogāsamarthaiśca sadyojātaiḥ śarīrakaiḥ 
te dṛṣṭvā tānsvayaṃbhūtānbrahmavyāhāriṇastadā  BndP 
saraṃbdhā vai vyakarṣanta mama putro mametyuta 
abhidhyāyātmanotpannānūcurvai te parasparam  BndP 
yo yasya vapuṣā tulyo bhajatāṃ satataṃ sutam 
yasya yaḥ sadṛśaścāpi rūpe vīrye ca mānataḥ  BndP 
taṃ gṛhṇātu sa bhadraṃ vo varṇato yasya yaḥ samaḥ 
dhruvaṃ rūpaṃ pituḥ putraḥ so 'nurudhyati sarvadā  BndP 
tasmādātmasamaḥ putraḥ piturmātuśca vīryataḥ 
evaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtvā sarveṣāṃ jagṛhaḥ sutān  BndP 
cākṣuṣasyāntare 'tīte prāpte vaivasvatasya ha 
ruceḥ prajāpateḥ putro raucyo nāmābhavatsutaḥ  BndP 
bhūtyāmutpādito yastu bhautyo nāma kaveḥ sutaḥ 
vaivasvateṃ'tare jātau dvau manū tu vivasvataḥ  BndP 
vaivasvato manuryaśca sāvarṇo yaśca vai śrutaḥ 
jñeyaḥ saṃjñāsuto vidvānmanurvaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ  BndP 
savarṇāyāḥ sutaścānyaḥ smṛto vaivasvato manuḥ 
sāvarṇama navo ye ca catvārastu maharṣijāḥ  BndP 
tapasā saṃbhṛtātmānaḥ sveṣu manvantareṣu vai 
bhaviṣyeṣu bhaviṣyanti sarvakāryārthasādhakāḥ  BndP 
prathame merusāvarṇedakṣaputrasya vai manoḥ 
parāmarīcigarbhāśca sudharmāṇaśca te trayaḥ 
saṃbhūtāśca mahātmānaḥ sarve vaivasvatentare  BndP 
dakṣaputrasya putrāste rohitasya prajāpateḥ 
bhaviṣyanti bhaviṣyāstu ekaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ  BndP 
aiśvaraśca graho rāhurvākurvaṃśastathaiva ca 
pārā dvādaśa vijñeyā uttarāṃstu nibodhata  BndP 
vājipo vājijiccaiva prabhūtiśca kakudyatha 
dadhikrāvā vipakvaśca praṇīto vijayo madhuḥ  BndP 
utathyottamakau dvau tu dvādaśaite marīcayaḥ 
sudharmāṇastu vakṣyāmi nāmatastānnibodhata  BndP 
varṇastathāthagarviśca bhuraṇyo vrajano 'mitaḥ 
amito dravaketuśca jaṃbho 'thājastu śakrakaḥ  BndP 
sunemirdyutayaścaiva sudharmāṇaḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
teṣāmindrastadā bhāvyo hyadbhuto nāma nāmataḥ  BndP 
skando 'sau pārvatīyo vai kārtikeyastu pāvakiḥ 
medhātithiśca paulastyo vasuḥ kāśyapa evaṃ ca  BndP 
jyotiṣmānbhārgavāścaiva dyutimānaṅgirāstathā 
vasinaścaiva vāsiṣṭha ātreyo havyavāhanaḥ  BndP 
sutapāḥ paulahaścaiva saptaite rohitetare 
dhṛtiketurdīptiketuḥ śāpahastanirāmayāḥ  BndP 
pṛthuśravāstathānīko bhūridyumno bṛhadyaśaḥ 
prathamasya tu sāvarṇernava putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BndP 
daśame tvatha paryāye dharmaputrasya vai manoḥ 
dvītīyasya tu sāvarṇerbhāvyasyaivāntare manoḥ  BndP 
sudhāmāno viruddhāśca dvāveva tu gaṇau smṛtau 
dīptimantaśca te sarve śatasaṃkhyāśca te samāḥ  BndP 
prāṇānāṃ yacchataṃ proktaṃ ṛṣibhiḥ puraṣeti vai 
devāste vai bhaviṣyanti dharmaputrasya vai manoḥ  BndP 
teṣāmindrastathā vidvānbhaviṣyaḥ śāntirucyate 
haviṣmānpaulahaḥ śrīmānsukīrtiścātha bhārgavaḥ  BndP 
āpomūrtistathātreyo vasiṣṭhaścāpavaḥ smṛtaḥ 
paulastyo 'pratimaścāpi nābhāgaścaiva kāśyapaḥ  BndP 
abhimanyuścāṅgirasaḥ saptaite paramarṣayaḥ 
sukṣetraścottamaujāśca bhūrisenaśca vīryavān  BndP 
śatānīko nirāmitro vṛṣaseno jayadrathaḥ 
bhūridyumnaḥ suvarcāśca daśaitemānavāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP 
ekādaśe tu paryāye sāvarṇe vai tṛtīyake 
nirvāṇaratayo devāḥ kāmagā vai manojavāḥ  BndP 
gaṇāstvete trayaḥ khyātā devātānāṃ mahātmanām 
ekaikastriṃśatasteṣāṃ gaṇastu tridivaukasām  BndP 
māsasyāhāni triṃśattu yāni vai kavayo viduḥ 
nirvāṇaratayo devā rātrayastu vihaṅgamāḥ  BndP 
gaṇastṛtīyo yaḥ prokte devatānāṃ bhaviṣyati 
manojavā mūrūrttāstu iti devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BndP 
ete hi brahmaṇaḥ putrā bhaviṣyā mānavāḥ smṛtāḥ 
teṣāmidro vṛṣā nāma bhaviṣyaḥ surarāṭ tataḥ  BndP 
teṣāṃ saptaṛṣīṃścāpi kīrtyamānānnivaudhata 
haviṣmānkāśyapaścāpi vapuṣmāṃścaiva bhārgavaḥ  BndP 
āruṇiśca tathātreyo vasiṣṭho naga eva ca 
puṣṭirāṅgiraso jñeyaḥ paulastyo niścarastathā  BndP 
paulaho hyatitejaśca devā hyekādaśentare 
sarvavegaḥ sudharmā ca devānīkaḥ purovahaḥ  BndP 
kṣemadharmā graheṣuśca ādarśaḥ paiṇḍrako maruḥ 
sāvarṇasya tu te putrāḥ prājāpatyasya vai nava  BndP 
dvādaśe tvatha paryāye rudraputrasya vai manoḥ 
caturtho rudrasāvarṇo devāṃstasyāntare śṛṇu  BndP 
pañcaiva tugaṇāḥ proktā devatānāmanāgatāḥ 
haritā rohitāścaiva devāḥ sumanasastathā  BndP 
sukarmāṇaḥ sutaraśca vidvāṃścaiva sahasradaḥ 
parvato 'nu caraścaiva apāśuśca manojavaḥ  BndP 
ūrjā svāhā svadhā tārā daśete haritāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tapo jñānī mṛtiścaiva varcā bandhuśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP 
rajaścaiva tu rājaśca svarṇapādastathaiva ca 
puṣṭirvidhiśca vai devā daśaite rohitāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP 
tuṣtādyāstu ye devāstraya striṃśatprakīrtitāḥ 
te vai sumanaso vedyānnibodhata sukarmaṇaḥ  BndP 
suparvā vṛṣabhaḥ pṛṣṭā kapidyumnavipaścitaḥ 
vikramaśca kramaścaiva vibhṛtaḥ kānta eva ca  BndP 
ete devāḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sutarāṃśca nibodhata 
varṣo divyastathāñjiṣṭho varcasvī dyutimānkaviḥ  BndP 
śubho haviḥ kṛtaprāptirvyāpṛto daśamastathā 
sutārā nāmatastvete devā vai saṃprakīrtitāḥ  BndP 
teṣāmindrastu vijñeyo ṛtadhāmā mahāyaśāḥ 
dyutirvasiṣṭhaputrastu ātreyaḥ sutapāstathā  BndP 
tapomūrtistvāṅgirasastapasvī kāśyapastathā 
tapodhanaśca paulastyaḥ paulahaśca taporatiḥ  BndP 
bhārgavaḥ saptamasteṣāṃ vijñeyastu tapodhṛtiḥ 
ete saptarṣayaḥ siddhā antye sāvarṇikeṃ'tare  BndP 
devavānupadevaśca devaśreṣṭho vidūrathaḥ 
mitravān mitraseno 'tha citraseno hyamitrahā  BndP 
mitrabāhuḥ suvarcāśca dvādaśasya manoḥ sutāḥ 
trayodaśetu paryāye bhāvye raucyentare punaḥ  BndP 
traya eva gaṇāḥ proktā devānāṃ tu svayaṃbhuvā 
brahmaṇo mānasāḥ putrāste hi sarve mahātmanaḥ  BndP 
sutrāmāṇaḥ sudharmāṇaḥ sukarmāṇaśca te trayaḥ 
tridaśānāṃ gaṇāḥ proktā bhaviṣyāḥ somapāyinām  BndP 
trayastriśaddevatā yāḥ pṛthagijyāstu yājñikaiḥ 
ājyena pṛṣadājyena grahaśreṣṭena caiva ha  BndP 
ye vai devāstrayastriṃśatpṛthaktvena nibodhata 
sutrāmāṇaḥ prayājyāstu ājyāśā ye tu sāṃpratam  BndP 
sukarmāṇo 'nuyājyākhyāḥ pṛṣadājyāśinastu ye 
upayājyāḥ sudharmāṇa iti devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ  BndP 
divaspatirmahāsatvasteṣāmindro bhaviṣyati 
pulahātmajaputrāste vijñeyāstu ruceḥ sutāḥ  BndP 
aṅgirāścaiva dhṛtimān paulastyo 'pyavyayastu saḥ 
paulahastattvadarśī cha bhārgavaśca nirupsukaḥ  BndP 
niṣprakaṃpyastathātreyo nirmohaḥ kāśyapastathā 
sutapāścaiva vāsiṣṭhaḥ saptaite tu trayodaśa  BndP 
citraseno vicitraśca nayo dharmo dhṛto bhavaḥ 
anekaḥ kṣatraviddhaśca suraso nirbhayo daśa  BndP 
raucyasyaite manoḥ putrā hyantare tu trayodaśe 
caturdaśe tu paryāye bhautyasyāpyantare manoḥ  BndP 
devatānāṃ gaṇāḥ pañca proktā ye tu bhaviṣyati 
cākṣuṣāśca pavitrāśca kaniṣṭhā bhrājitāstathā  BndP 
vācāvṛddhāśca ityete pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ 
niṣādādyāḥ svarāḥ sapta sapta tānviddhi cākṣuṣān  BndP 
bṛhadādyāni sāmāni kaniṣṭhānsapta tānviduḥ 
sapta lokāḥ pavitrāste bhrājitāḥ saptasiṃdhavaḥ  BndP 
vācāvṛddhānṛṣīnviddhi manoḥ svāyabhuvasya ye 
sarve manvantaredrāśca vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ  BndP 
tejasā tapasā vuddhyā balaśrutaparākramaiḥ 
trailokye yāni sattvāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca  BndP 
sarvaśaḥ sarvairguṇaistāni indrāste 'bhibhavanti vai 
bhūtāpavādino hṛṣṭā madhyasthā bhūtavādinaḥ  BndP 
bhūtābhavādinaḥ śaktāstrayo vedāḥ pravādinām 
agnīdhraḥ kāśyapaścaiva paulastyo māgadhaśca yaḥ  BndP 
bhārgavo hyagnivāhuśca śucirāṅgirasastathā 
śukraścaiva tu vāsiṣṭhaḥ paulaho mukta eva ca  BndP 
ātreyaḥ śvājitaḥ prokto manuputrānataḥ śṛṇu 
ururguruśca gaṃbhīro buddhaḥ śuddhaḥ śuciḥ kṛtī  BndP 
ūrjasvī subalaścaiva bhautyasyaite manoḥ sutāḥ 
sāvarṇā manavo hyete catvāro brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ  BndP 
eko vaivasvataścaiva sāvarṇo manurucyate 
raucyo bhautyaśca yau tau tu matau paulahabhārgavau 
bhautyasyaivādhipatye tu tūrṇaṃ kalpastu pūryate  BndP 
sūta uvāca
niḥśeṣeṣu tu sarveṣu tadā manvantareṣviha  BndP 
ante 'nekayuge tasminkṣīṇe saṃhāra ucyate 
saptaite bhārgavā devā ante manvantare tadā  BndP 
bhuktvā trailokyama dhyasthā yugākhyā hyekasaptatīḥ 
pitṛbhirmanubhiḥ sārddhaṃ kṣīṇe manvantare tadā  BndP 
anādhāramidaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ vai bhaviṣyati 
tataḥ sthānā ni śubhrāṇi sthānināṃ tāni vai tadā  BndP 
prabhraśayante vimuktāni tārā ṛkṣagrahaistathā 
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu trailokyasyeśvareṣviha  BndP 
saṃprapteṣu maharlokaṃ yasmiṃste kalpavāsinaḥ 
ajitādyā gaṇā yatra āyuṣmantaścaturdaśa  BndP 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu devāste vai caturddaśa 
saśarīrāśca śrūyante janaloke sahānugāḥ  BndP 
evaṃ deveṣvatīteṣu maharlokājjanaṃ prati 
bhūtādiṣvavaśiṣṭeṣu sthāvarāṃ teṣu teṣu vai  BndP 
śūnyeṣu lokasthāneṣu mahānteṣu bhuvādiṣu 
deveṣu ca gateṣvūrddhvaṃ sāyujyaṃ kalpavāsinām  BndP 
saṃhṛtya tāstato brahmā devarṣipitṛdānavān 
saṃsthāpayati vai sargamahardṛṣṭvā yugakṣaye  BndP 
caturyugasahasrāntamaharyadbrahmaṇo viduḥ 
rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ te 'horātravido janāḥ  BndP 
naimittikaḥ prākṛtiko yaścaivātyantikor'thataḥ 
trividhiḥ sarvabhūtānāmityeṣa pratisaṃcaraḥ  BndP 
brāhmo naimittikastasya kalpadāhaḥ prasaṃyamaḥ 
pratisarge tu bhūtānāṃ prākṛtaḥ karaṇakṣayaḥ  BndP 
jñānāccātyantikaḥ proktaḥ kāraṇānāmasaṃbhavaḥ 
tataḥ saṃhṛtya tānbrahmā devāṃstrailokyavāsinaḥ  BndP 
praharati prakurute sargasya pralayaṃ punaḥ 
suṣupsurbhagavānbrahmā prajāḥ saṃharate tadā  BndP 
tato yugasahasrānte saṃprāpte ca yugakṣaye 
tatrātmasthāḥ prajāḥ kartuṃ prapede sa prajāpatiḥ  BndP 
tadā bhavatyanāvṛṣṭiḥ saṃtatā śatavārṣikī 
tayā yānyalpasārāṇi sattvāni vṛthivītale  BndP 
tānyevātra pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca

divasya sūryo 'dhipatistena sūryo divaspatiḥ  BndP

janastu pañcamo lokastasmājjāyanti vai janāḥ 
tāsāṃ svāyaṃbhuvādyānāṃ prajānāṃ jananājjanaḥ  BndP

kalpa ete yadā loke pratiṣṭhanti tadā tapaḥ  BndP

prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve varttaṃnne tatra taiḥ saha

bhūmyantaraṃ yadādityādantarikṣaṃ bhuvaḥ smṛtam

dhruvājjanāntaraṃ yacca maharlokaḥ sa ucyate

bhuvi svarge ca ye sarve somapā ājyapāśca te  BndP

vāyuruvāca

pulastyaḥ pulahaschaiva kraturityevāmādayaḥ

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ

sūta uvāca
śṛṇudhvaṃ me parārddhasya parisaṃkhyāṃ parasyaca  BndP

vijñeyamāsahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇi daśāyutam  BndP

tathā śatasahasrāṇāṃ daśaprayutamucyate  BndP 
tathā daśasahasrāṇāmayutaṃ koṭirucyate 
arbudaṃ daśakoṭyastu hyabjaṃ koṭiśataṃ viduḥ  BndP 
sahasramāpi koṭīnāṃ kharvamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ 
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi nikharvamiti taṃ viduḥ  BndP

vijñeyamayutaṃ tasmānniyutaṃ prayutaṃ tataḥ  BndP

evamaṣṭādaśaitāni sthānāni gaṇanāvidhau  BndP

āveśyātmani tānsarvān saṃkhyāyogyabhavāṃstathā  BndP 
lokānsapta imānbhūyo mahābhūtāni pañca ca 
viṣṇunā saha saṃyuktaḥ karoti vikaroti ca  BndP 
sa rudro yaḥ sāmamayastathaiva ca yajurmayaḥ 
sa eṣa otaḥ protaśca bahirantaśca niścayāt  BndP 
eko hi bhagavānnāthaḥ prabhavaścāntakṛddvijāḥ 
tataste ṛṣayaḥ sarve divākarasamaprabhāḥ  BndP 
susatyaṃ śravasaḥ samyagāropyāgniṃ tathātmani 
karmaṇā manasā vācā viśuddhenāntarātmanā  BndP 
ananyamanaso bhūtvā prapadyante maheśvaram 
vratopavāsaniratāḥ sarvabhūtadayāparāḥ  BndP 
yogaṃ tvanuyamaṃ divyaṃ prāptantaiśchinnasaṃśayaiḥ 
prapadya parayā bhaktyājñānayuktena tejasā  BndP 
tairlabdhaṃ rudrasālokyaṃ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam 
yaḥ paṭhettapasā yukto vāyuproktāmimāṃ śrutim  BndP 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpivaiśyo vā svakriyāparaḥ 
labhate rudralokaṃ vai kāraṇaṃ lokakāraṇam  BndP 
vinivṛtte tadā sarge prakṛtyā vasthitena vai 
tadātyantaparokṣatvādadṛṣṭatvācca kasyacit  BndP 
anākhyānādabodhyatvādajñānājjñānināmapi 
āgatāgatikatvācca grahaṇaṃ tanna vidyate  BndP 
bhāvagrāhyānumānācca cintayitvedamucyate 
sthite tu kāraṇe tasminnitye sadasadātmake  BndP 
anirdeśye pravṛttirvai svātmikākāraṇena tu 
evaṃ saptadvirabhyastāḥ kramātprakṛtayastu vai  BndP 
pratyāhāre tadā sarge praviśanti parasparam 
yenedamāvṛtaṃ sarvamaṇḍamapsu pralīyate  BndP 
saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptalokaṃ saparvatam 
udakāvaraṇaṃ yacca jyotiṣyālīyate tu yat  BndP 
yattejasaṃ cāvaraṇaṃ māruto grasate nu yat 
yadvāyavyaṃ cāvaraṇamākāśagrasate tu tat  BndP 
ākāśāvaraṇaṃ yacca bhūtādirgrasate tu tat 
bhūtādiṃ grasate cāpi mahānvai buddhilakṣamaḥ  BndP 
mahāntaṃ grasate 'vyaktaṃ guṇasāmyaṃ tataḥ param 
etau saṃhāravistārau brahmā vyaktau tataḥ punaḥ  BndP 
sṛjate grasate caiva vikārātsargasaṃyame 
saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇāḥ saṃsiddhā jñāninastu ye  BndP 
gatvā javaṃ javībhāve sthāne sveṣu prasaṃyamāt 
pratyāhāre 'dhiyujyante kṣetrajñāḥ karaṇaiḥ punaḥ  BndP 
avyaktaṃ kṣetramityāhurbrahmā kṣetrajña ucyate 
sādharmyavaidharmyakṛtaḥ saṃyogo nādimāstayoḥ  BndP 
evaṃ sargeṣu vijñeyaḥ kṣetrajñeṣviha brāhmaṇāḥ 
brahmaviccaiva vijñeyaḥ kṣetrajñānātpṛthak  BndP 
viṣayāviṣayatvaṃ ca kṣetrakṣetrajñayoḥ smṛtam 
brahmā tvaviṣayo jñeyo viṣayaḥ kṣetramucyate  BndP 
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñārthaṃ pracakṣate 
bahutvācca śarīrāṇāṃ śarīrī bahudhā smṛtaḥ  BndP 
avyūhāśaṅkarāccaiva jyotiryacca vyavasthitam 
yasmātpratiśarīraṃ hi sukhaduḥkho palabdhitā  BndP 
tasmātpuruṣanānātvaṃ vijñeyaṃ tu vijānatā 
yadā pravarttate caiṣāṃ bhedānāṃ caiva saṃyamaḥ  BndP 
svabhāvakāritāḥ sarve kālena mahatā tadā 
nivarttante tadā tasminsthitarāgāḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ  BndP 
saha sāyujyakaiḥ sarvairbrahmalokanivāsibhiḥ 
vinivṛttestadā teṣāṃ sthiterātmanivāsinām  BndP 
tatkālavāsināṃ teṣāṃ tatra vai doṣadarśinām 
utpadyate 'tha vairāgyamātmavāda praṇāśanam  BndP 
bhojyabhoktṛtvanānātvaisteṣāṃ tadbhāvadarśinām 
pṛthagjñānena kṣetrajñāstataste brahmalaukikāḥ  BndP 
prakṛtau kāraṇātītāḥ sarve nānāpradarśinaḥ 
svātmanyevāvatiṣṭhante praśāntādarśanātmakāḥ  BndP 
śuddhā nirañjanāḥ sarve cetanācetanāstathā 
tatraiva parinirvāṇāḥ smṛtānāgāminastu te  BndP 
nirguṇatvāgnirātmānaḥ prakṛtyante vyatikramāt 
ityevaṃ prākṛtaḥ proktaḥ pratisargaḥ svayaṃbhuvā  BndP 
varṇāśramācārayutaḥ pratisargaṃ śṛṇoti yaḥ 
sa vrajecchivasālokyaṃ bhaktimānvigatajvaraḥ  BndP 
amadyapaśca ya śūdro bhavabhakto jitedriyaḥ 
ābhūtasaṃplavasthāyī apratīghātalakṣaṇaḥ  BndP 
gāṇapatyaṃ sa labhate sthānaṃ vā sārvakālikam 
madyapo madyapaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhūtasaṃghaiśca modate  BndP 
sevyamāno mahīpṛṣṭhe martyānāṃ varado bhavaḥ 
iti hovāca bhagavānvāyurvākyamidavaram  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte uttarabhāge caturtha upasaṃhārapāde śivapuravarṇanaṃ nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
pratyāhāraṃ pravakṣyāmi parasyānte svayaṃbhuvaḥ 
brahmaṇaḥ sthitikāle tu kṣīṇe tasmiṃstadā prabhoḥ  BndP 
yathedaṃ kurute vyaktaṃ susūkṣmaṃ viśvamīśvaraḥ 
avyaktaṃ grasate vyaktaṃ pratyāhāre ca kṛtsnaśaḥ  BndP 
purāntadvyaṇukādyānāṃ saṃpūrṇe kalpasaṃkṣaye 
upasthite mahāghore hyapratyakṣe tu kasyacit  BndP 
ante drumasya saṃprāpte paścimāsya manostadā 
ante kaliyuge tasminkṣīṇe saṃhāra ucyate  BndP 
saṃprakṣāle tadā vṛtte pratyāhāre hyupasthite 
pratyāhāre tadā tasminbhūtatanmātrasaṃkṣaye  BndP 
mahadādivikārasya viśeṣāntasya saṃkṣaye 
svabhāvakārite tasminpravṛtte pratisaṃcare  BndP 
āpo grasaṃti vai pūrvaṃ bhūmergandhātmakaṃ gumam 
āttagandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayatvāya kalpate  BndP 
praṇaṣṭe gandhatanmātre toyāvasthā dharā bhavet 
āpastadā praviṣṭāstu vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ  BndP 
sarvamāpūrayitvedaṃ tiṣṭhanti vicaranti ca 
apāmapi gaṇo yastu jyotiḥṣvālīyate rasaḥ  BndP 
naśyantyāpastadā tatra rasatanmātrasaṃkṣayāt 
tīvratejohṛtarasājyotiṣṭvaṃ prāpnuvantyuta  BndP 
graste ca salile tejaḥ sarvatomukhamīkṣate 
athāgniḥ sarvato vyāpta ādatte tajjalaṃ tadā  BndP 
sarvamāpūryate 'rcirbhistadā jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ 
arcirbhiḥ saṃtate tasmiṃstaryagūrdhvamadhastataḥ  BndP 
jyotiṣo 'pi guṇaṃ rūpaṃ vāyuratti prakāśakam 
pralīyate tadā tasmindīpārciriva mārute  BndP 
pranaṣṭe rūpatanmātre hṛtarūpo vibhāvasuḥ 
upaśāmyati tejo hivāyurādhūyate mahān  BndP 
nirāloke tadā loke vāyubhūte ca tejasi 
tatastu mūlamāsādya vāyuḥ saṃbandhamātmanaḥ  BndP 
ūrdhvañcādhaśca tiryakca dodhavīti diśo daśa 
vāyorapi guṇaṃ sparśamākāśaṃ grasate ca tat  BndP 
praśāmyati tadā vāyuḥ khantu tiṣṭhatyanāvṛtam 
arūpamarasasparśamagandhaṃ na ca mūrtimat  BndP 
sarvamāpūrayacchabdaiḥ sumahattatprakāśate 
tasmiṃllīne tadā śiṣṭamākāśaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam  BndP 
śabdamātraṃ tadākāśaṃ sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati 
tatra śabdaṃ gumaṃ tasya bhūtadirgrasate punaḥ  BndP 
bhūtendriyeṣu yugapadbhūtādau saṃsthiteṣu vai 
abhimānātmako hyeṣa bhūtādistāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP 
bhūtādirgrasate cāpi mahānvai buddhilakṣaṇaḥ 
mahānātmā tu vijñeyaḥ saṃkalpo vyavasāyakaḥ  BndP 
buddhirmanaśca liṅgaṃ ca mahānakṣara eva ca 
paryāyavācakaiḥ śabdaistamāhustattva cintakāḥ  BndP 
saṃpralīneṣu bhūteṣu guṇasāmye tato mahān 
līyante guṇasāmyaṃ tu svātmanyevāvatiṣṭhate  BndP 
līyante sarvabhūtānāṃ kāraṇāni prasaṃgame 
ityeṣa saṃyamaścaiva tattvānāṃ kāraṇaiḥ saha  BndP 
tattvaprasaṃyamo hyeṣa smṛto hyāvartako dvijāḥ 
dharmādharmauṃ tapo jñānaṃ śubhaṃ satyānṛte tathā  BndP 
ūrdhvabhāvo hyadhobhāvaḥ sukhaduḥkhe priyāpriye 
sarvametatprapañcasthaṃ guṇamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam  BndP 
nirindriyāṇāṃ ca tadā jñānināṃ yacchubhāśubham 
prakṛtyāṃ caiva tatsarvaṃ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ pratiṣṭhati  BndP 
yātyavasthā tu sācaiva dehināṃ tu nirucyate 
jantūnāṃ pāpapuṇyaṃ tu prakṛtau yatpratiṣṭhitam  BndP 
avasthāsthāni tānyeva puṇyapāpāni jantavaḥ 
yojayante punardehānparatvena tathaiva ca  BndP 
dharmādharmauṃ tu jantūnāṃ guṇamātrātmakāvubhau 
kāraṇaiḥ svaiḥ pracīyete kāyatveneha jantubhiḥ  BndP 
sacetanāḥ pralīyante kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitā guṇāḥ 
sarge ca pratisarge ca saṃsāre caiva jantavaḥ  BndP 
saṃyujyante viyujyante kāraṇaiḥ saṃcaranti ca 
rājasī tāmasī caiva sāttvikī caiva vṛttayaḥ  BndP 
guṇamātrāḥ pravartante puruṣādhiṣṭhatā stridhā 
urddhvadeśātmakaṃ sattvamadhobhāgātmakaṃ tamaḥ  BndP 
tayoḥ pravarttakaṃ madhye ihaivāvarttakaṃ rajaḥ 
ityevaṃ parivartantetrayaścetoguṇātmakāḥ  BndP 
lokeṣu sarvabhūtānāṃ tanna kāryaṃ vijānatā 
avidyāpratyayāraṃbhā ārabhyante hi mānavaiḥ  BndP 
etāstu gatayastisraḥ śubhātpāpātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tamaso 'bhibhavājjanturyāthātathyaṃ na vindati  BndP 
atattvadarśanātso 'tha vividhaṃ vadhyate tataḥ 
prākṛtena ca bandhena tathyāvaikārikeṇa ca  BndP 
dakṣiṇābhistatīyena baddho 'tyantaṃ vivarttate 
ityete vai trayaḥ proktā bandhā hyajñānahetukāḥ  BndP 
anitye nityasaṃjñā ca duḥkhe ca sukhadarśanam 
asve svamiti ca jñānamaśucau śuciniścayaḥ  BndP 
yeṣāmete manodoṣā jñānadoṣā viparyayāt 
rāgadveṣanivṛttiśca tajjñānaṃ samudāhṛtam  BndP 
ajñānaṃ tamaso mūraṃ karmadvayaphalaṃ rajaḥ 
karma jastu punardeho mahāduḥkhaṃ pravarttate  BndP 
śrotrajā netrajā caiva tvagjihvāghrāṇajā tathā 
punarbhavakarī duḥkhātkarmaṇā jāyate tṛṣā  BndP 
satṛṣṇo 'bhihito bālaḥ svakṛtaiḥ karmaṇaḥ phalaiḥ 
tailavīḍakavajjīvastatraiva parivarttate  BndP 
tasmānmūlamanarthānāmajñāna mupadiśyate 
taṃ śatrumavadhāryaikaṃ jñāne yatnaṃ samācaret  BndP 
jñānāddhi tyajate sarvaṃ tyāgādbuddhirvirajyate 
vairāgyācchudhyate cāpi śuddhaḥ sattvena mucyate  BndP 
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi rāgaṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam 
abhiṣvaṅgāya yogaḥ syādviṣayeṣvavaśātmanaḥ  BndP 
aniṣṭamiṣṭamaprītiprītitāpaviṣādanam 
duḥkhalābhe na tāpaśca sukhānusmaraṇaṃ tathā  BndP 
ityeṣa vaiṣayo rāgaḥ saṃbhūtyāḥ kāraṇaṃ smṛtaḥ 
brahmādau sthāvarānte vai saṃsārehyādibhautike  BndP 
ajñānapūrvakaṃ tasmādajñānaṃ tu vivarjayet 
yasya cārṣe na pramāṇaṃ śiṣṭācāraṃ tathaiva ca  BndP 
varṇāśramaviruddho yaḥ śiṣṭaśāstravirodhakaḥ 
eṣa mārgo hi niraye tiryyagyonau ca kāraṇam  BndP 
tiryyagyo nigataṃ caiva kāraṇaṃ tattrarucyate 
trividho yātanāsthāne tiryyagyonau ca ṣaḍvidhe  BndP 
kāraṇe viṣaye caiva pratighātastu sarvaśaḥ 
anaiśvaryaṃ tu tatsarvaṃ pratighātātmakaṃ smṛtam  BndP 
ityeṣā tāmasī vṛttirbhūtādīnāṃ caturvidhā 
sattvasthamātrakaṃ cittaṃ yathāsattvaṃ pradarśanāt  BndP 
tattvānāṃ ca yathātattvaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai tattvadarśanāt 
sattvakṣetrajñanānātvametannānārthadarśanam  BndP 
nānātvadarśanaṃ jñānaṃ jñānādvai yoga ucyate 
tena baddhasya vai bandho mokṣo muktasya tena ca  BndP 
saṃsāre vinivṛtte tu mukto liṅgena mucyate 
niḥsaṃbandho hyacaitanyaḥ svātmanyevāvatiṣṭhate  BndP 
svātmanyavasthitaścāpi virūpākhyena likhyate 
ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ samāsājjñāna mokṣayoḥ  BndP 
sa cāpi trividhaḥ prokto mokṣo vai tattvadarśibhiḥ 
pūrvaṃ viyogo jñānena dvitīye rāgasaṃkṣayāt  BndP 
tṛṣṇākṣa yāttṛtīyastu vyākhyātaṃ mokṣakāraṇam 
liṅgābhāvāttu kaivalyaṃ kaivalyāttu nirañjanam  BndP 
nirañjanatvācchuddhastu nitānyo naiva vidyate 
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vairāgyaṃ doṣadarśanāt  BndP 
divye ca mānuṣe caiva viṣaye pañcalakṣaṇe 
apradveṣo 'nabhiṣvaṅgaḥ karttavyo doṣadarśanāt  BndP 
tapaprītiviṣādānāṃ kāryaṃ tu parivarjanam 
evaṃ vairāgyamāsthāya śarīrī nirmamo bhavet  BndP 
anityamaśivaṃ duḥkhamiti vuddhyānucintya ca 
viśuddhaṃ kāryakaraṇaṃ sattvasyātiniṣaivayā  BndP 
paripakvakaṣāyo hi kṛtsnāndoṣānprapaśyati 
tataḥ prayāṇakāle hi doṣairnaimittikaistathā  BndP 
ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥ 
sa śarīramupāśritya kṛtsnāndoṣānruṇaddhi vai  BndP 
prāṇakthānāni bhindanhi chindanmarmāṇyatītya ca 
śaityātprakupito vāyurūrddhvaṃ tūtkramate tataḥ  BndP 
sa cāyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prāṇasthāneṣvavasthitaḥ 
samāsātsaṃvṛte jñāne saṃcṛtteṣu ca karmasu  BndP 
sa jīvo nābhyadhiṣṭhānaḥ karmabhiḥ svaiḥ purākṛtaiḥ 
aṣṭāṅgapraṇavṛttiṃ vai sa vicyāvayate punaḥ  BndP 
śarīraṃ prajahansoṃ'te nirucchvāsastato bhavet 
evaṃ prāṇaiḥ parityakto mṛta ityabhidhīyate  BndP 
yatheha loke svapne taṃ nīyamānamitastataḥ 
rañjanaṃ tadvidheyasya te tānyo na ca vidyate  BndP 
nṛṣṇākṣayastṛtīyastu vyākhyātaṃ mokṣalakṣaṇam 
śabdādye viṣaye doṣadṛṣṭirvai pañcalakṣaṇe  BndP 
apradveṣo 'nabhiṣvaṅgaḥ prītitāpavivarjanam 
vairāgyakāraṇaṃ hyete prakṛtīnāṃ layasya ca  BndP 
aṣṭau prakṛtayo jñeyāḥ pūrvoktā vai yathākramam 
avyaktādyāstu vijñeyā bhūtāntāḥ prakṛterbhavāḥ  BndP 
varṇāśramācārayuktaḥ śiṣṭaḥ śāstrāvirodhanaḥ 
varṇāśramāṇāṃ dharmo 'yaṃ devasthāneṣu kāraṇam  BndP 
brahmādīni piśācāntānyaṣṭau sthānāni devatā 
aiśvaryamāṇimādyaṃ hi kāraṇaṃ hyaṣṭalakṣaṇam  BndP 
nimittamapratīghāte dṛṣṭe śabdādilakṣaṇe 
aṣṭāvetāni rūpāṇi prākṛtāni yathākramam  BndP 
kṣetrajñeṣvanusajjante guṇamātratmakāni tu 
prāvṛṭkāle pṛthagmeghaṃ paśyantīva sacakṣuṣaḥ  BndP 
paśyantyevaṃ vidhāḥ siddhā jīvaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā 
khādataścānnapānāni yonīḥ praviśatastathā  BndP 
tiryagūrdhvamadhastācca dhāvato 'pi yathākramam 
jīvaḥ prāṇastathā liṅgaṃ karaṇaṃ ca catuṣṭayam  BndP 
paryāyavācakaiḥ śabdairekārthaiḥ so 'bhilaṣyate 
vyaktāvyaktapramāṇo 'yaṃ sa vai bhuṅkte tu kṛtsnaśaḥ  BndP 
avyaktānugrahāntaṃ ca kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ ca yat 
evaṃ jñātvā śucirbhūtvā jñānādvai vipramucyate  BndP 
naṣṭaṃ caiva yathā tattvaṃ tattvānāṃ tattvadarśane 
yatheṣṭaṃ pariniryāti bhinne dehe sunirvṛte  BndP 
bhidyate karaṇaṃ cāpi hyavyaktajñāninastataḥ 
mukto guṇaśarīreṇa praṇādyena tu sarvaśaḥ  BndP 
nānyaccharīramādatte dagdhe vīje yathāṅkuraḥ 
jñānī ca sarvasaṃsārāvijñaśārīramānasaḥ  BndP 
jñānāccaturddaśābuddhaḥ prakṛtistho nivartate 
prakṛtiṃ satyamityāhurvikāro 'nṛtamucyate  BndP 
asadbhāvo 'nṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ sadbhāvaḥ satya mucyate 
anāmarūpaṃ kṣetrajñanāmarūpaṃ pracakṣate  BndP 
yasmātkṣetraṃ vijānāti tatmātkṣetrajña ucyate 
kṣetraṃ pratyayate yasmātkṣetrajñaḥ śubha ucyate  BndP 
kṣetrajñaḥ smaryate tasmātkṣetraṃ tajjñairvibhāṣyate 
kṣetraṃ tvatpratyayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kṣetrajñaḥ pratyayaḥ sadā  BndP 
kṣapaṇātkāraṇāccaiva kṣatatrāṇāttathaiva ca 
bhojyatvaviṣayatvācca kṣetraṃ kṣetravido viduḥ  BndP 
mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ sarvairūpyaṃ vilakṣaṇam 
vikāralakṣaṇaṃ tadvai so 'kṣaraḥ kṣarameti ca  BndP 
tamevānuvikāraṃ tu yasmādvai kṣarate punaḥ 
tasmācca kāraṇāccaiva jñaramityabhidhīyate  BndP 
saṃsāre narakebhyaśca trāyate puruṣaṃ ca yat 
duḥkhatrāṇātpunaścāpi kṣetramityabhidhīyate  BndP 
sukhaduḥkhamahaṃbhāvādbhojyamityabhidhīyate 
acetanatvādviṣayastadvidharmā vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP 
na kṣīyate na kṣarati vikāraprasṛtaṃ tu tat 
akṣaraṃ tena vāpyuktama kṣīṇatvāttathaiva ca  BndP 
yasmātpūryanuśete ca tasmātpuruṣa ucyate 
purapratyayiko yasmātpuruṣetyabhidhīyate  BndP 
puruṣaṃ kathayasvātha kathito 'jñairvibhāṣyate 
śuddho nirañjanābhāso jñātā jñānavivarjitaḥ  BndP 
astināstīti so 'nyo vā baddho mukto gataḥsthitaḥ 
nairhetukāttvanirdeśyādahastasminna vidyate  BndP 
śuddhatvānna tu dṛśyo vai draṣṭṛtvātsamadarśanaḥ 
ātmapratyayakāritvādanyūnaṃ vāpyahetukam  BndP 
bhāvagrāhyamanumānāccintayanna pramuhyate 
yadā paśyati jñātāraṃ śāntārthaṃ darśanātmakam  BndP 
dṛśyādṛśyeṣu nirdeśyaṃ tadā taddurddharaṃ varam 
vijñātā na ca dṛśyeta vṛthaktveneha sarvaśaḥ  BndP 
svenātmanā tathātmānaṃ kāraṇātmā niyacchati 
prakṛtau kāraṇe tatra svātmanyevopatiṣṭhati  BndP 
astināstīti so 'nyo vā ihāmutreti vā punaḥ 
ekatvaṃ vā pṛthakvaṃ vā kṣetrajñaḥ puruṣo 'pi vā  BndP 
ātmā vā sa nirātmā vā cetano 'cetano 'pi vā 
karttā vā so 'pyakarttā vā bhoktā vā bhojyameva ca  BndP 
yadgatvā na nivarttante kṣetrajñaṃ tu nirañjanam 
avācyaṃ tadanākhyānādagrāhyaṃ vādahetubhiḥ  BndP 
apratarkyamacintyatvādavā yetvācca sarvaśaḥ 
nālapya vacasā tattvamaprāpya manasā saha  BndP 
kṣetrajñe nirguṇe śuddhe śānte kṣīṇe nirañjane 
vyapetasukhaduḥkhe ca niruddhe śāntimāgate  BndP 
nirātmake punastasminvācyāvācyaṃ na vidyate 
etau saṃhāravistārau vyaktāvyaktau tataḥ punaḥ  BndP 
sṛjyate grasate caiva vyaktau paryavatiṣṭhate 
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ punaḥ sarge pravarttate  BndP 
adhiṣṭhānaṃ prapadyeta tasyānte buddhipūrvakam 
sādharmyavaidharmyakṛtaḥ saṃyogo viditastayoḥ 
anādimāṃśca saṃyogo mahāpuruṣajaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP 
yāvacca sargaprati sargakālastāvajjagattiṣṭhati saṃnirudhya 
pūrvaṃ hi tasyaiva ca buddhipūrvaṃ pravarttate tatpuruṣārthaṃmeva  BndP 
eṣā nisargapratisargapūrvā prādhānikī ceśvarakāritā vā 
anādyanantā hyabhimānapūrvakaṃ vitrāsayantī jagadabhyupaiti  BndP 
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargastṛtīyo hetulakṣaṇaḥ 
ukto hyasmiṃstadātyantaṃ kālaṃ jñātvā pramucyate  BndP 
ityeṣa pratisargo vastrividaḥ kīrttito mayā 
vistareṇānupūrvyāca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varttayāmyaham  BndP 
iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte uttarabhāge caturtha upasaṃhārapāde pratisargo nāma tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrutaṃ sumahadākhyānaṃ bhavatā parikīrttitam 
prajānāṃ manubhiḥ sārddhaṃ devānāmṛṣibhiḥ saha  BndP 
pitṛgandharvabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām 
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca yakṣāṇāmeva pakṣiṇām  BndP 
atyadbhutāni karmāṇi vividhā dharmaniścayāḥ 
vicitrāśca kathāyogā janma cāgryamanuttamam  BndP 
tatkathyamānamasmākaṃ bhavatā ślakṣṇayā girā 
manaḥ karṇasukhaṃ saute prīṇātyamṛtasannibham  BndP 
evamārādhya te sūtaṃ satkṛtya ca maharṣayaḥ 
papracchuḥ sattriṇaḥ sarve punaḥ sargapravarttanam  BndP 
kathaṃ suta mahāprājña punaḥ sargaḥ prapatsyate 
bandheṣu saṃpralīneṣu guṇasāmye tamomaye  BndP 
vikāreṣvavisṛṣṭeṣu hyavyakte cātmani sthite 
apravṛtte brahmaṇā tu sahasā yojyagaistadā  BndP 
kathaṃ prapatsyate sargastannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām 
evamuktastataḥ sūtastadāsau lomaharṣaṇaḥ  BndP 
vyākhyātumupacakrāma punaḥ sargapravarttanam 
atra vo varttayiṣyāmi yathā sargaḥ prapatsyate  BndP 
pūrvavatsa tu vijñeyaḥ samāsāttannibodhata 
dṛṣṭenaivānumeyaṃ ca tarkaṃ vakṣyāmi yuktitaḥ  BndP 
yasmādvāco nivarttante tvaprāpya manasā saha 
avyakta vatparokṣatvādgahanaṃ taddurāsadam  BndP 
vikāraiḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭo guṇaḥ sāmyena varttate 
pradhānaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ ca sādharmyeṇaiva tiṣṭhati  BndP 
dharmādharmauṃ pralīyete hyavyakte prāṇināṃ sadā 
sattvamātrātmako dharmo guṇe sattve pratiṣṭhitaḥ  BndP 
tamomātrātmako dharmo guṇe tamasi tiṣṭhati 
avibhāgena tāvetau guṇasāmye sthitāvubhau  BndP 
sarvaṃ kāryaṃ buddhipūrvaṃ pradhānasya prapatsyate 
buddhipūrvaṃ kṣetrajña adhiṣṭhāsyati tānguṇān  BndP 
evaṃ tānabhimānena prapatsyati punastadā 
yadā pravarttitavyaṃ tu kṣetrakṣetrajñayor dvayoḥ  BndP 
bhojyabhoktṛtvasaṃbandhāḥ prapatsyante ca tāvubhau 
tasmādakṣaramavyaktaṃ sāmye sthitvā guṇātmakam  BndP 
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ tatra vaipamyaṃ bhajate tu tat 
tataḥ prapatsyate vyaktaṃ kṣetrakṣetrajñayordvayoḥ  BndP 
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ sattvaṃ vikāraṃ janayiṣyati 
mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ caturviṃśaguṇātmakam  BndP 
kṣetrajñasya pradhānasya puruṣasya pravartsyataḥ 
ādidevaḥ pradhānasyānugrahāya prajakṣate  BndP 
anādyau varamutpādau ubhau sūkṣmau tu tau smṛtau 
anādisaṃyogayutau sarvaṃ kṣetrajñameva ca  BndP 
abuddhipūrvakaṃ yuktamāśaktau tu varau tadā 
apratyayamamoghaṃ ca sthitāvudakamatsyavat  BndP 
pravṛttapūrvauṃ tau pūrvaṃ punaḥ sarvaṃ prapatsyate 
ajñā guṇaiḥ pravarttante rajaḥsattvatamo 'bhidhaiḥ  BndP 
pravṛttikāle rajasābhipanno mahattvabhūtādiviśeṣatāṃ ca 
viśeṣatāṃ cendriyatāṃ ca yāti guṇāvasānauṣadhibhirmanuṣyaḥ  BndP 
satyābhidhyāyinastasya dhyāyinaḥ sannimittakam 
rajaḥ sattvatamovyaktā vidharmāṇaḥ parasparam  BndP 
ādyantaṃ vai pravatsyante kṣetramajñāmvu sarvaśaḥ 
saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇā utpadyante 'bhimāninaḥ  BndP 
sarve sattvāḥ prapadyante hyavyaktātpūrvameva ca 
prāksṛtau ye tvasuvahāḥ sādhakāścāpyasādhakāḥ  BndP 
asaṃśāntāstu te sarve sthānaprakaraṇaiḥ saha 
kāryāṇi pratipatsyante utpatsyante punaḥ punaḥ  BndP 
guṇamātrātmakāveva dharmādharmauṃ parasparam 
ārapsaṃte hi cānyonyaṃ vareṇānugraheṇa vā  BndP 
śarvastulyaprasṛṣṭyartha sargādau yāti vikriyām 
guṇāstaṃ pratidhīyante tasmāttattasya rocate  BndP 
guṇāste yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭyāṃ pratipedire 
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ  BndP 
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte 
tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate  BndP 
mahābhūteṣu nānātvamindriyārtheṣu mūrttiṣu

ityeṣa vo mayā khyātaḥ punaḥ sargaḥ samāsataḥ 
samāsādeva vakṣyāmi brahmaṇo 'tha samudbhavam  BndP 
avyaktātkāraṇāttasmānnityātsadasadātmakāt 
pradhānapuruṣābhyāṃ tu jāyate ca maheśvaraḥ  BndP

sṛjate sa punarlokānabhimāna guṇātmakān  BndP

yathā yūyaṃ vidhinā devātādīniṣṭvā caivāvabhṛthaṃ prāpya śuddhāḥ 
tyaktvā dehānāyuṣoṃ'te kṛtārthāḥ puṇyaṃ lokaṃ prāpya modadhvamevam  BndP 
ete te naimiṣeyā vai dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā ca vai tadā 
jagmuścāvabhṛthasnātāḥ svargaṃ sarve tu satriṇaḥ  BndP 
viprāstathā yūyamapi iṣṭā bahuvidhairmakhaiḥ 
āyuṣoṃ'te tataḥ svargaṃ gantāraḥ stha dvijottamāḥ  BndP 
prakriyā prathamaḥ pādaḥ kathāyāstu parigrahaḥ 
anuṣaṅga upoddhāta upasaṃhāra eva ca  BndP 
evameva catuḥpādaṃ purāṇaṃ lokasammatam 
uvāca bhāgavānsakṣādvāyulokahite rataḥ  BndP 
naimiṣe satramā sādya munibhyo munisattama 
tatprasādaṃ ca saṃsiddhaṃ bhūtotpattilayānvitam  BndP 
prādhānikīmimāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ tathaiveśvarakāritām 
samyagviditvā medhāvī na mohamadhigacchati  BndP 
idaṃ yo brāhmaṇo vidvānitihāsaṃ purātanam 
śṛṇuyācchrāvayedvāpi tathādhyāpayate 'pi ca  BndP 
sthāneṣu sa mahendrasya modate śāśvatīḥ samāḥ 
brahmasāyujyago bhūtvā brahmaṇā saha modate  BndP 
teṣāṃ kīrtimatāṃ kīrtiṃ prajeśānāṃ mahātmanām 
prathayanpṛthivīśānāṃ brahmabhūyāya gacchati  BndP 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiśca saṃmitam 
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanenoktaṃ purāṇa brahmavādinā  BndP 
manvantareśvarāṇāṃ ca yaḥ kīrtiṃ prathayedimām 
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca bhūridravimatejasām  BndP 
sa sarvairmucyate pāpaiḥ puṇyaṃ ca mahadāpnuyāt 
yaścedaṃ śrāvayedvidvānsadā parvaṇi parvaṇi  BndP 
dhūtapāpmā jitasvargo brahmabhūyāya kalpate

akṣeyaṃ sarvakāmīyaṃ pitṝṃstacchopatiṣṭhate

niruktamasya yo veda sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
tathaiva triṣu varṇeṣu ye manuṣyā adhīyate  BndP 
itihāsamimaṃ śrutvā dharmāya vidadhe matim 
yāvantyasya śarīreṣu romakūpāni sarvaśaḥ  BndP 
tāvatkoṭisahasrāṇi varṣāṇi divi modate 
brahmasāyujyago bhūtvā daivataiḥ saha modate  BndP 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ ca yaśasvi ca 
brahmā dadau śāstramidaṃ purāṇaṃ mātariśvane  BndP 
tasmāccośanasā prāptaṃ tasmāccāpi bṛhaspatiḥ 
bṛhaspatistu provāca savitre tadanantaram  BndP 
savitā mṛtyave prāha mṛtyuścendrāya vai punaḥ 
indraścāpi vasiṣṭhāya so 'pi sārasvatāya ca  BndP 
sārasvatastridhāmne 'tha tridhāmā ca śaradvate 
śaradvāṃstu triviṣṭāya soṃ'tarikṣāya dattavān  BndP 
carṣiṇe cāntarikṣo vai so 'pi trayyāruṇāya ca 
trayyāruṇāddhanañjayaḥ sa vai prādātkṛtañjaye  BndP 
kṛtañjayāttṛṇañjayo bharadvājāya so 'pyatha 
gautamāya bharadvājaḥ so 'pi niryyantare punaḥ  BndP 
niryyantarastu provāca tathā vājaśravāya vai 
sa dadau somaśuṣmāya sa cādāttṛṇabindave  BndP 
tṛṇabindustu dakṣāya dakṣaḥ provāca śaktaye 
śakteḥ parāśaraścāpi garbhasthaḥ śrutavānidam  BndP 
parāśarājjātukarṇyastasmāddvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ 
dvaipāyanā tpunaścāpi mayā prāptaṃ dvijottama  BndP 
mayā caitatpunaḥ proktaṃ putrāyāmitabuddhaye 
ityeva vākyaṃ brahmādiguruṇāṃ samudātdṛtam  BndP 
namaskāryāśca guravaḥ prayatnena manīṣibhiḥ 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvārthasādhakam  BndP 
pāpaghnaṃ niyamenedaṃ śrotavyaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ sadā 
nāśucau nāpi pāpāya nāpyasaṃvatsaroṣite  BndP 
nāśraddadhāne 'viduṣe nāputrāya kathañcana 
nāhitāya pradātavyaṃ pavitramidamuttamam  BndP 
avyaktaṃ vai yasya yoniṃ vadanti vyaktaṃ dehaṃ kālametaṃ gatiṃ ca 
vahnirvaktraṃ candrasūryauṃ ca netrediśaḥ śrotre ghrāṇamāhuśca vāyum  BndP 
vāco vedā antarikṣaṃ śarīraṃ kṣitiḥ pādāstārakā romakūpāḥ 
sarvāṇi dyaurmastakāni tvatho vai vidyāścaivopaniṣadyasya puccham  BndP 
taṃ devadevaṃ jananaṃ janānāṃ yajñātmakaṃ satyalokapratiṣṭham 
varaṃ varāṇāṃ varadaṃ maheśvaraṃ brahmāṇamādiṃ prayato namasye  BndP 
 iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte dvādaśasāharsyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ uttarabhāge caturthaṃ upasaṃhārapāde brahmāṇḍāvarttaṃ nāma caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ 
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ 
atha śrīlalitopākhyānaṃ prārabhyate 
caturbhuje candrakalāvataṃse kuconnate kuṅkumarāgaśoṇe 
puṇḍrekṣupāśāṅkuśapuṣpabāṇahaste namaste jagadekamātaḥ  BndP 
astu naḥ śreyase nityaṃ vastu vāmāṅgasundaram 
yatastṛtīyo viduṣāṃ tṛtīyastu paraṃ mahaḥ  BndP 
agastyo nāma devarṣirvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ 
sarvasiddhāntasārajño brahmānandarasātmakaḥ  BndP 
cacārādbhutahetūni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca 
śailāraṇyāpagāmukhyānsarvāñjanapadānapi  BndP 
teṣu teṣvakhilāñjantūnajñānatimirāvṛtān 
śiśnodaraparāndṛṣṭvā cintayāmāsa tānprati  BndP 
tasya cintayamānasya carato vasudhāmimām 
prāptamāsīnmahāpuṇyaṃ kāñcīnagaramuttamam  BndP 
tatra vāraṇaśailenadramekāmranilayaṃ śivam 
kāmākṣīṃ karidoṣadhnīmapūjayadathātmavān  BndP 
lokahetordayārdrasya dhīmataścintano muhuḥ 
cirakālena tapasā toṣito 'bhūjjanārdanaḥ  BndP 
hayagrīvāṃ tanuṃ kṛtvā sākṣāccinmātravigrahām 
śaṅkhacakrākṣavalayapustakojjvalabāhukām  BndP 
pūrayitrīṃ jagatkṛtsnaṃ prabhayā dehajātayā 
prādurbabhūva purato muneramitatejasā  BndP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvānandabharitaḥ praṇamya ca muhurmuhuḥ 
vinayāvanato bhūtvā santuṣṭāva jagatpatim  BndP 
athovāca jagannāthastuṣṭo 'smi tapasā tava 
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te bhavitā bhūsurottamaḥ  BndP 
iti pṛṣṭo bhagavatā provāca munisattamaḥ 
yadi tuṣṭo 'si bhagavannime pāmarajantavaḥ  BndP 
kenopāyena muktāḥ syuretanme vaktumarhasi 
iti pṛṣṭo dvijenātha devadevo janārdanaḥ  BndP 
eṣa eva purā praśnaḥ śivena carito mama 
ayameva kṛtaḥ praśno brahmaṇā tu tataḥ param  BndP 
kṛto durvāsasā paścādbhavatā tu tataḥ param  BndP 
bhavadbhiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ gurubhūtairmahātmabhiḥ 
mamopadeśo lokeṣu prathito 'stu varo mama  BndP 
ahamādirhi bhūtānāmādikartā svayaṃ prabhuḥ 
sṛṣṭisthitilayānāṃ tu sarveṣāmapi kārakaḥ  BndP 
trimūrtistriguṇātīto guṇahīno guṇāśrayaḥ  BndP 
icchāvihāro bhūtātmā pradhānapuruṣātmakaḥ 
evaṃ bhūtasya me brahmaṃstrijagadrūpadhāriṇaḥ  BndP 
dvidhākṛtamabhūdrūpaṃ pradhāna puruṣātmakam 
mama pradhānaṃ yadrūpaṃ sarvalokaguṇātmakam  BndP 
aparaṃ yadguṇātītaṃ parātparataraṃ mahat 
evameva tayorjñātvā mucyate te ubhe kimu  BndP 
tapobhiścirakālotthairyamaiśca niyamairapi 
tyāgairduṣkarmanāśānte muktirāśveva labhyate  BndP 
yadrūpaṃ yadguṇayutaṃ tadguṇyaikyena labhyate 
anyatsarvajagadrūpaṃ karmabhogaparākramam  BndP 
karmabhirlabhyate tacca tattyāgenāpi labhyate 
dustarastu tayostyāgaḥ sakalairapi tāpasa  BndP 
anapāyaṃ ca sugamaṃ sadasatkarmagocaram  BndP 
ātmasthena guṇenaiva satā cāpyasatāpivā 
ātmaikyenaiva yajjñānaṃ sarvasiddhigradāyakam  BndP 
varṇatrayavihīnānāṃ pāpiṣṭhānāṃ nṛṇāmapi 
yadrūpadhyānamātreṇa duṣkṛtaṃ sukṛtāyate  BndP 
yer'cayanti parāṃ śaktiṃ vidhināvidhināpi vā 
na te saṃsāriṇo nūnaṃ muktā eva na saṃśayaḥ  BndP 
śivo vā yāṃ samārādhya dhyānayogabalena ca 
īśvaraḥ sarvasiddhānāmarddhanārīśvaro 'bhavat  BndP 
anye 'bjapramukhā devāḥ siddhāstaddhyānavaibhavāt

na sto bhogāpavargauṃ tu yaugapadyena kutracit

tādātmyenaiva karmāṇi kurvanmuktimavāpsyasi 
etadrahasyamākhyātaṃ sarveṣāṃ hitakāmyayā  BndP 
santuṣṭenaiva tapasā bhavato munisattama

iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā hayagrīvasya śārṅgiṇaḥ 
praṇipatya punarvākyamuvāca madhusūdanam  BndP 
bhagavankīdṛśaṃ rūpaṃ bhavatā yatpuroditam 
kiṃvihāraṃ kiṃprabhāvametanme vaktumarhasi  BndP 
hayagrīva uvāca
eṣoṃ'śabhūto devarṣe hayagrīvo mamāparaḥ 
śrotumicchasiyadyattvaṃ tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhati  BndP 
ityādiśya jagannātho hayagrīvaṃ tapodhanam 
purataḥ kumbhajātasya munerantaradhāddhariḥ  BndP 
tatastu vismayāviṣṭo hṛṣṭaromā tapodhanaḥ 
hayagrīveṇa muninā svāśramaṃ pratyapadyata  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne agastyayātrājanārdanāvirbhāvo nāma pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ
athopaveśya caivainamāsane paramādbhute 
hayānanamupāgatyāgastyo vākyaṃ samabravīt  BndP 
bhagavansarvadharmajña sarvasiddhāntavittam

āvirbhāvaṃ mahādevyāstasyā rūpāntarāṇi ca 
vihāraścaiva mukhyā ye tānno vistarato vada  BndP 
hayagrīva uvāca
anādirakhilādhārā sadasatkarmarūpiṇī 
dhyānaikadṛśyā dhyānāṅgī vidyāṅgī hṛdayāspadā  BndP 
ātmaikyādvyaktimāyāti cirānuṣṭhānagauravāt  BndP

prakṛtirnāma sā khyātā devānāmiṣṭasiddhidā  BndP 
dvitīyamudabhūdrūpaṃ pravṛtte 'mṛtamanthane

visṛjya pārvatīṃ śīghrantayā ruddho 'tanodratam  BndP 
tasyāṃ vai janayāmāsa śāstāramasurārdanam  BndP 
agastya uvāca
kathaṃ vai sarvabhūteśo vaśī manmatha śāsanaḥ 
aho vimohito devyā janayāmāsa cātmajam  BndP 
hayagrīva uvāca
purāmarapurādhīśo vijayaśrīsamṛddhimān 
trailokyaṃ pālayāmāsa sadevāsuramānuṣam  BndP

aśobhano hyatejasko mama śāpādbhaviṣyati  BndP

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devendrasya bṛhaspatiḥ 
pratyuvāca tato vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ śubham  BndP

prāyaścittopabhogābhyāṃ vinā nāśo na jāyate  BndP

bṛhaspatiruvāca
hananasteyahiṃsāśca pānamanyāṅganāratiḥ 
karma pañcavidhaṃ prāhurduṣkṛtaṃ dharaṇīpateḥ  BndP 
brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdragoturaṅgakharoṣṭrakāḥ

daśapañcatrirekārdhamānupūrvyādidaṃ bhavet  BndP 
brahmakṣatraviśāṃ strīṇāmuktārthe pāpamādiśet

gurvājñayā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tadājñālaṅghaner'thakam 
daśabrāhmaṇabhṛtyarthamekaṃ hanyāddvijaṃ nṛpaḥ  BndP 
śatabrāhmaṇabhṛtyarthaṃ brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ tu vā 
pañcabrahmavidāmarthe traiśyamekaṃ tu daṇḍayet  BndP 
vaiśyaṃ daśaviśāmarthe viśāṃ vā daṇḍayettathā 
tathā śataviśāmarthe dvijamekaṃ tu daṇḍayet  BndP 
śūdrāṇāṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ daṇḍayedbrāhmaṇaṃ tu vā 
tacchatārthaṃ tu vā vaiśyaṃ taddaśārddhaṃ tu śūdrakam  BndP 
bandhūnāṃ caiva mitrāṇāmiṣṭārthe tu tripādakam 
arthaṃ kalatraputrārthe svātmārthe na tu kiñcana  BndP 
ātmānaṃ hantumārabdhaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyaṃ viśam

tatastu paramā śaktirbhūtasaṃdhasahāyinī

anena turagaṃ gā vā gajoṣṭramahiṣādikam

viśvasya hatvā pāpiṣṭhaṃ śūdraṃ vāpyantyajātijam

yo hanyādavicāreṇa so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  BndP

tadgopanaṃ niśārdhāyāṃ tasmindūraṃ gate sati  BndP

jahārāviditastena kāṣṭhabhāraṃ vahanyayau  BndP

māṃ vilokyaivamacirādbahubhāgyavatī bhavet  BndP

tathāpi bahubhāgyānāṃ puṇyānāmapi pātriṇe

atha vātmaprayāsena kṛcchrādyallabhyate dhanam

svayamāgatavittaṃ tu dharmārthairviniyojayet

dvijavarmeti nāmāsmai tasyai śīlavatīti ca

purohitābhidhānena devarātapurantviti

anyo 'nyamabhavatteṣāṃ yuddhaṃ devāsuropamam

gateṣvakhiladūteṣu śrutvā nāradabhāṣitam

bhāryāṃ tasyāha sa munistava doṣo na kiñcana

tatastu yā gatistasya tāmevānucarāmyaham 
parihāro 'thavā kiṃ tu mayā kāryastu tena vā  BndP 
iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā prītaḥ prāha tapodhanaḥ 
bhogātmakaṃ śarīraṃ tu karma kāryakaraṃ tava  BndP 
mama prabhāvādbhavitā parihāraṃ vadāmi te

pūjayitvā śivaṃ bhaktyā kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ 
dhyātvā hṛdi maheśānaṃ śatarudramanuṃ japet  BndP

pāpairanyaiśca sakalairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  BndP 
ityādiśya dadau tasyai rudrādhyāyaṃ tapodhanaḥ 
anugṛhyeti tāṃ nārīṃ tatraivāntarddhimāgamat  BndP

vimuktasteyadoṣeṇa svaśarīramavāpa saḥ  BndP

anye taddravyavanto 'pi kāladharmamupāgatāḥ  BndP 
yamastu tānsamāhūya vākyaṃ caitaduvāca ha  BndP 
bhavadbhistu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ daivātsukṛtamapyuta 
kimicchatha phalaṃ bhoktuṃ duṣkṛtasya śubhasya vā  BndP 
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā procurvajrādikāstataḥ 
sukṛtasya phalaṃ tvādau paścātpāpasya bhujyate  BndP 
punarāha yamo yūyaṃ putramitra kalatrakaiḥ 
etasyaiva balātsarve tridivaṃ gacchata drutam  BndP 
te 'dhiruhya vimānāgryaṃ dvijavarmāṇamāśritāḥ 
yathocitaphalopetāstridivaṃ jagmurañjasā  BndP 
dvijavarmākhilāṃllokānatītya pramadāsakhaḥ

iti brahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne steyapānakathanaṃ nāma saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ
indra uvāca
agamyāgamanaṃ kiṃ vā ko doṣaḥ kā ca niṣkṛtiḥ 
etanme muniśārdūla vistarādvaktumarhasi  BndP

agamyāgamanaṃ nāma mātṛsvasṛgurustriyaḥ

indra uvāca
bhagavansarvadharmajña sarvabhūtahite rata

bṛhaspatiruvāca
saṃyogajaṃ tu yatpāpaṃ taccaturdhā nigadyate 
kartā pradhānaḥ sahakṛnnimitto 'numataḥ kramāt  BndP 
kramāddaśāṃśato 'ghaṃ syācchuddhiḥ pūrvoktamārgataḥ  BndP 
madyaṃ kalañjaṃ niryāsaṃ chatrākaṃ gṛñjanaṃ tathā

biṃbīṃ ca kavakaṃ caiva hastinīṃ śiśulaṃbikām

athavā śaṅkaraṃ dhyāyañjaptvā traiyyaṃbakaṃ manum

idaṃ rahasyaṃ devendra śṛṇuṣva vacanaṃ mama

nāsyānnadoṣajaṃ kiñcinna dāridrayabhayaṃ tathā  BndP

prāyaścittaṃ tathā teṣāṃ kimanyacchrotumicchasi  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne 'ṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ
indra uvāca
bhagavansarva dharmajña trikālajñānavittama

kena karmavipākena mamāpadi yamāgatā 
prāyaścittaṃ ca kiṃ tasya gadasva vadatāṃ vara  BndP 
bṛhaspatiruvāca
kāśyapasya tato jajñe dityāṃ danuriti smṛtaḥ 
kanyā rūpavatī nāma dhātre tāṃ pradadau pitā  BndP 
tasyāḥ putrastato jāto viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥ 
nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ  BndP

karmabhūmiṃ vrajeḥ śīghraṃ dārirdyeṇa mitaiḥ sutaiḥ 
evaṃ prakupitaiḥ śaptaḥ khinnaḥ kāñcīṃ samāviśam  BndP

babhūvatustulyabalau tadā detyendravāsavau  BndP

śirāṃsi yaugapadyena chinnātyāsaṃstvayaiva tu  BndP 
tena pāpena saṃyuktaḥ pīḍitaśca muhurmuhuḥ

putra śokena saṃtaptastvāṃ śaśāpa ruṣānvitaḥ  BndP

anāthakāstato devā viṣaṇṇā daityapīḍitāḥ  BndP

tadaghaṃ tu tridhā bhittvā triṣu sthāneṣvathārpayat

tadā bharttṛsamāyogaṃ putrāvāptimṛtuṣvapi 
chede punarbhavatvaṃ tu sarveṣāmapi śākhinām  BndP

teṣvaghaṃ prababhūvāśu rajoniryāsamūṣaram  BndP

rājyaśriyaṃ ca saṃprāptaḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ  BndP 
tenaiva sāṃtvito dhātā jagāda ca janārdanam 
mama śāpo vṛthā na syādastu kālāntare mune  BndP 
bhagavāṃstadvacaḥ śrutvā muneramitatejasaḥ 
prahṛṣṭo bhāvikāryajñastūṣṇīmeva tadā yayau  BndP 
etāvantamimaṃ kālaṃ trilokīṃ pālayanbhavān

na yajñāḥ saṃpravarttante na dānāni ca vāsava

hayagrīva uvāca
itthaṃ kathayatoreva bṛhaspatipahendrayoḥ 
malakādyā mahādaityāḥ svargalokaṃ babādhire  BndP 
nandanodyāna makhilaṃ cicchidurbalagarvitāḥ 
udyānapālakānsarvānāyudhaiḥ samatāḍayan  BndP

ājahurapsaroratnānyaśeṣāṇi viśeṣataḥ 
tato devāḥ samastāśca cakrurbhṛśamabādhitāḥ  BndP

sarvairanugato devaiḥ palāyanaparo 'bhavat  BndP

yathāvatkathayāmāsa nikhilaṃ daityaceṣṭitam  BndP 
vidhātāpi tadākarṇya sarvadevasamanvitam 
hataśrīkaṃ harihayamālokyedamuvāca ha  BndP 
indratvamakhilairddevairmukundaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja 
daityārātirjagatkartā sa te śreyo vidhāsyati  BndP 
ityuktvā tena sahitaḥ svayaṃ brahmā pitāmahaḥ 
samastadevasahitaḥ kṣīrodadhimupāyayau  BndP 
atha brahmādayo devā bhagavantaṃ janārdanam 
tuṣṭuvurvāgvariṣṭhābhiḥ sarvalokamaheśvaram  BndP 
atha prasanno bhagavānvāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ 
jagāda sa kalāndevāñjagadrakṣaṇalaṃpaṭaḥ  BndP 
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhavatāṃ suvidhāsyāmi tejasaivopabṛṃhamam 
yaducyate mayedānīṃ yuṣmābhista dvidhīyatām  BndP 
oṣadhipravarāḥ sarvāḥ kṣipata kṣīrasāgare 
asurairapi saṃdhāya samameva ca tairiha  BndP 
manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā yoktraṃ ca vāsukim 
mayi sthite sahāye tu mathyatāmamṛtaṃ surāḥ  BndP 
samastadānavāścāpi vaktavyāḥ sāṃtvapūrvakam 
sāmānyameva yuṣmākamasmākaṃ ca phalaṃ tviti  BndP 
mathyamāne tu dugdhābdhau yā samutpadyate sudhā 
tatpānādbalino yūyamamartyāśca bhaviṣyatha  BndP 
yathā daityāśca pīyūṣaṃ naitatprāpsyanti kiñcana 
kevalaṃ kleśavantaśca kariṣyāmi tathā hyaham  BndP 
iti śrīvāsudevena kathitā nikhilāḥ surāḥ 
saṃdhānaṃ tvatulairdaityaiḥ kṛtavantastadā surāḥ 
nānāvidhauṣadhigaṇaṃ samānīya surāsurāḥ  BndP 
śrīrābdhipayasi kṣiptvā candramo 'dhikanirmalam 
manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā yoktraṃ tu vāsukim 
prārebhire prayatnena manthituṃ yādasāṃ patim  BndP 
vāsukeḥ pucchabhāge tu sahitāḥ sarvadevatāḥ 
śirobhāge tu daiteyā niyuktāstatra śauriṇā  BndP 
balavanto 'pi te daityāstanmukhocchvāsapāvakaiḥ 
nirdagdhavapuṣaḥ sarve nistejaskāstadābhavan  BndP 
pucchadeśe tu karṣanto muhurāpyāyitāḥ surāḥ 
anukūlena vātena viṣṇunā preritena tu  BndP 
ādikūrmākṛtiḥ śrīmānmadhye kṣīrapayonidheḥ 
bhramato mandarādrestu tasyā dhiṣṭānatāmagāt  BndP 
madhye ca sarvadevānāṃ rūpeṇānyena mādhavaḥ 
cakarṣa vāsukiṃ vegāddaityamadhye pareṇa ca  BndP 
brahmarūpeṇa taṃ śailaṃ vidhāryākrāntavāridhim 
apareṇa ca devarṣirmahatā tejasā muhuḥ  BndP 
upavṛṃhitavāndevānyena te balaśālinaḥ 
tejasā punaranyena balātkārasahena saḥ  BndP 
upabṛṃhitavānnāgaṃ sarvaśaktijanārdanaḥ 
mathyamāne tatastasminkṣīrabdhau devadānavaiḥ  BndP 
āvirbabhūva purataḥ surabhiḥ surapūjitā 
mudaṃ jagmustadā devā daiteyāśca tapodhana  BndP 
mathyamāne punastasminkṣīrābdau devadānavaiḥ 
kimetaditi siddhānāṃ divi cintayatāṃ tadā  BndP 
utthitā vāruṇī devī madāllolavilocanā 
asurāṇāṃ purastātsā smayamānā vyatiṣṭhata  BndP 
jagṛhurnaiva tāṃ daityā asurāścābhavaṃstataḥ 
surā na vidyate yeṣāṃ tenaivāsuraśabditāḥ  BndP 
athasā sarvadevānāmagrataḥ samatiṣṭhata 
jagṛhustāṃ mudā devāḥ sūcitāḥ parameṣṭhinā 
surāgrahaṇato 'pyete suraśabdena kīrtitāḥ  BndP 
mathyamāne tato bhūyaḥ pārijāto mahādrumaḥ 
āvirāsītsuṃgadhena parito vāsayañjagat  BndP 
atyarthasuṃdarākārā dhīrāścāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ 
āvirbhūtāśca devarṣe sarvalokamanoharāḥ  BndP 
tataḥ śītāṃśurudabhūttaṃ jagrāha maheśvaraḥ 
viṣajātaṃ tadutpannaṃ jagṛhurnāgajātayaḥ  BndP 
kaustubhākhyaṃ tato ratnamādade tajjanārdanaḥ 
tataḥ svapatragandhena madayantī mahauṣadhīḥ 
vijayā nāma saṃjajñe bhairavastāmupādade  BndP 
tato divyāṃbaradharo devo dhanvantariḥ svayam 
upasthitaḥ kare bibhradamṛtāḍhyaṃ kamaṇḍalum  BndP 
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanaso devā daityāśca sarvataḥ 
munayaścābhavaṃstuṣṭāstadānīṃ tapasāṃ nidhe  BndP 
tato vikasitāṃbhojavāsinī varadāyinī 
utthitā padmahastā śrīstasmātkṣīramahārmavāt  BndP 
atha tāṃ munayaḥ sarve śrīsuktena śriyaṃ parām 
tuṣṭuvustuṣṭa hṛdayā gandharvāśca jaguḥ param  BndP 
viśvājīpramukhāḥ sarve nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ 
gaṅgādyāḥ puṇyanadyaśca snānārthamupatasthire  BndP 
aṣṭau digdantinaścaiva medhyapātrasthitaṃ jalam 
ādāya snāpayāñcakrustāṃ śriyaṃ padmavāsinīm  BndP 
tulasīṃ ca samutpannāṃ parārdhyā maikyajāṃ hareḥ 
padmamālāṃ dadau tasyai mūrtimānkṣīrasāgaraḥ  BndP 
bhūṣaṇāni ca divyāni viśvakarmā samarpayat 
divyamālyāṃ baradharā divyabhūṣaṇabhūṣitā 
yayau vakṣasthalaṃ viṣṇoḥ sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ ramā  BndP 
tulasī tu dhṛtā tena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā 
paśyati sma ca sā devī viṣṇuvakṣathalālayā 
devāndayārdrayā dṛṣṭyā sarvalokamaheśvarī  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne amṛtamanthanaṃ nāma navamo 'dhyāyaḥ
hayagrīva uvāca
atha devā mahendrādyā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣmunā 
aṅgīkṛtā mahādhīrāḥ pramodaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ  BndP 
malakādyāstu te sarve daityā viṣṇuparāṅmukhāḥ 
saṃtyaktāśca śriyā devyā bhṛśamudvegamāgatāḥ  BndP 
tato jagṛhire daityā dhanvantarikarasthitam 
paramāmṛtasārāḍhyaṃ kalaśaṃ kanakodbhavam 
athāsurāṇāṃ devānāmanyonyaṃ kalaho 'bhavat  BndP 
etasminnantare viṣṇuḥ sarvalokaikarakṣakaḥ 
samyagārādhayāmāsalalitāṃ svaikyarūpiṇīm  BndP 
surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca raṇaṃ vīkṣya sudāruṇam 
brahmā nijapadaṃ prāpa śaṃbhuḥ kailāsamāsthitaḥ  BndP 
malakaṃ yodhayāmāsa daityānāmadhipaṃ vṛṣā 
asuraiśca surāḥ sarve sāṃparāyamakurvata  BndP 
bhagavānapi yogīndraḥ samārādhya maheśvarīm 
tadekadhyānayogena tadrūpaḥ samajāyata  BndP 
sarvasaṃmohinī sā tu sākṣācchṛṅgāranāyikā 
sarvaśṛṅgāraveṣāḍhyā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā  BndP 
surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca nivārya raṇamulvaṇam 
mandasmitena daiteyānmohayantī jagada ha  BndP 
alaṃ yuddhena kiṃ śastrermarmasthānavibhedibhiḥ 
niṣṭhuraiḥ kiṃ vṛthālāpaiḥ kaṇṭhaśoṣaṇahetubhiḥ  BndP 
ahamevātra madhyasthā yuṣmākaṃ ca divaukasām 
yūyaṃ tathāmī nitarāmatra hi kleśabhāginaḥ  BndP 
sarveṣāṃ samamevādya dāsyāmyamṛtamadbhutam 
mama haste pradātavyaṃ sudhāpātramanuttamam  BndP

pīyūṣakalaśaṃ tasyai daduste mugdhacetasaḥ  BndP

dvayoḥ paṅktyośca madhyasthāstānuvāca surāsurān

tadvākyamurarīcakruste sarve samavāyinaḥ 
sā tu saṃmohitāśleṣalokā dātuṃ pracakrame  BndP 
kvaṇatkanakadarvīkā kvaṇanmaṅgalakaṅkaṇā 
kamanīyavibhūṣāḍhyā kalā sā paramā babhau  BndP

diśantī kramaśāstatra candrabhāskarasūcitam

pītāmṛtaśiromātraṃ tasya vyoma jagāma ca  BndP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvāpyasurāstatra tūṣṇīmāsanvimohitāḥ 
evaṃ krameṇa tatsarvaṃ vibudhebhyo vitīrya sā 
asurāṇāṃ puraḥ pātraṃ sānināya tirodadhe  BndP 
riktapātraṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve daiteyadānavāḥ 
udvelaṃ kevalaṃ krodhaṃ prāptā yuddhacikīrṣayā  BndP 
indrādayaḥ surāḥ sarve sudhāpānādbalottarāḥ 
durvalairasuraiḥ sārdhaṃ samayuddhyanta sāyudhāḥ  BndP

digantānkaticijjagmuḥ pātālaṃ katicidyayuḥ  BndP

kṛtvā tāmeva madhyasthāmarpayāmāsurañjasā  BndP

sarvasaṃmohajanakamavāṅmanasagocaram

yaddhyānavaibhavāllabdhaṃ rūpamadvaitamadbhutam  BndP

samāptaścopoddhātakhaṇḍaḥ 
agastya uvāca
kathaṃ bhaṇḍāsuro jātaḥ kathaṃ vā tripurāṃbikā 
kathaṃ babhañja taṃ saṃkhye tatsarvaṃ vada vistarāt  BndP 
hayagrīva uvāca
purā dākṣāyaṇīṃ tyaktvā pituryajñavināśanam  BndP 
ātmānamātmanā paśyañjñānānandarasātmakaḥ 
upāsyamāno munibhiradvandvaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ  BndP 
gaṅgākūle himavataḥ paryante praviveśa ha 
sāpi śaṅkaramā rādhya cirakālaṃ manasvinī  BndP 
yogena svāṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā sutāsīddhimabhūbhṛtaḥ  BndP

etasminnantare devāstārakeṇa hi pīḍitāḥ 
brahmaṇoktāḥ samāhūya madanaṃ cedamabruvan  BndP 
sargādau bhagavānbrahma sṛjamāno 'khilāḥ prajāḥ 
na nirvṛtirabhūttasya kadācidapi mānase

brahmovāca 
yadi tuṣṭo 'si bhagavannanāyāsena vai jagat 
carācarayutaṃ caitatsṛjāmi tvatprasādataḥ  BndP 
evamukto vidhātrā tu mahāla kṣmīmudaikṣata 
tadā prādurabhūstvaṃ hi jaganmohanarūpadhṛk  BndP 
tavāyudhārthaṃ dattaṃ ca puṣpabāṇekṣukārmukam 
vijayatvamajeyatvaṃ prādā tpramudito hariḥ  BndP 
asau sṛjati bhūtāni kāraṇena svakarmaṇā 
sākṣibhūtaḥ svajanato bhavānbhajatu nirvṛntim  BndP 
eṣa dattavaro brahmā tvayi vinyasya tadbharam 
manaso nirvṛtiṃ prāpya vartate 'dyāpi manmatha  BndP 
amoghaṃ balavīryaṃ te na te moghaḥ parākramaḥ  BndP 
sukumārāṇyamoghāni kusumāstrāṇi te sadā 
brahmadattavaro 'yaṃ hi tārako nāma dānavaḥ  BndP 
bādhate sakalāṃllokānasmānapi viśeṣataḥ 
śivaputrādṛte 'nyatra na bhayaṃ tasya vidyate  BndP 
tvāṃ vināsminmahākārye na kaścitpravadedapi 
svakarācca bhavetkāryaṃ bhavato nānyataḥ kvacit  BndP 
ātmyaikyadhayānanirataḥ śivo gauryā samanvitaḥ 
himācalatale ramye vartate munibhirvṛtaḥ  BndP 
taṃ niyojaya gauryāṃ tu janiṣyati ca tatsutaḥ 
īṣatkāryamidaṃ kṛtvā trāyasvāsmānmahābala  BndP 
evamabhyarthito devaiḥ stūyamāno muhurmuhuḥ 
jagāmātmavināśāya yato himavatastaṭam  BndP 
kimapyārādhayāntaṃ tu dhyānasaṃmīlitekṣaṇam 
dadarśeśānamāsīnaṃ kusumaṣurudāyudhaḥ  BndP 
etasminnantare tatra himavattanayā śivam 
ārirādhayiṣuścā gādbibhrāṇā rūpamadbhutam  BndP 
sametya śambhuṃ girijāṃ gandhapuṣpopahārakaiḥ 
śuśrūṣaṇaparāṃ tatra dadarśātibalaḥ smaraḥ  BndP 
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānānnātidūre 'sya saṃsthitaḥ 
sumanomārgaṇairagryaissa vivyādha maheśvaram  BndP 
vismṛtya sa hi kāryāṇi bāṇaviddho 'ntike sthitām 
gaurīṃ vilokayāmāsa manmathāviṣṭacetanaḥ  BndP 
dhṛtimālaṃbya tu punaḥ kimetaditi cintayan 
dadarśāgre tu sannaddhaṃ manmathaṃ kusumāyudham  BndP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā kupitaḥ śūlī trailokyadahanakṣamaḥ 
tārtīyaṃ cakṣurunmīlya dadāha makaradhvajam  BndP 
śivenaivamavajñātā duḥkhitā śailakanyakā 
anujñayā tataḥ pitrostapaḥ kartumagādvanam  BndP 
atha tadbhasma saṃvīkṣya citrakarmā gaṇeśvaraḥ 
tadbhasmanā tu puruṣaṃ citrākāraṃ cakāra saḥ  BndP 
taṃ vicitratanuṃ rudro dadarśāgre tu pūruṣam 
tatkṣaṇājjāta jīvo 'bhūnmūrtimāniva manmathaḥ 
mahābalo 'titejasvī madhyāhnārkasamaprabhaḥ  BndP 
taṃ citrakarmā bāhubhyāṃ samāliṅgya mudānvitaḥ 
stuhi vāla mahādevaṃ sa tu sarvārthasiddhidaḥ  BndP 
ityuktvā śatarudrīyamupādiśadameyadhīḥ 
nanāma śataśo rudraṃ śatarudriyamājapan  BndP 
tataḥ prasanno bhagavānmahādevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa varaṃ vavre sa bālakaḥ  BndP 
pratidvandvibalārthaṃ tu madbalenopayokṣyati 
tadastraśastramukhyāni vṛthā kurvantu no mama  BndP 
tatheti tatpratiśrutya vicārya kimapi prabhuḥ 
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi rājyamasmai dadau punaḥ  BndP 
etaddṛṣṭvā tu caritaṃ dhātā bhaṇḍiti bhaṇḍiti 
yaduvāca tato nāmnā bhaṇḍo lokeṣu kathyate  BndP 
iti dattvā varaṃ tasmai sarvairmunigaṇairvṛtaḥ 
dattvāstrāṇi ca śastrāṇi tatraivāntaradhācca saḥ  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne bhaṇḍāsuraprādurbhāvo nāmaikādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
rudrakopānalājjāto yato bhaṇḍo mahābalaḥ 
tasmādraudrasvabhāvo hi dānavaścābhavattataḥ  BndP 
athāgacchanmahātejāḥ śukro daityapurohitaḥ 
samāyātāśca śataśo daiteyāḥ sumahābalāḥ  BndP 
athāhūya mayaṃ bhaṇḍo daityavaṃśyādiśilpinam 
niyukto bhṛguputreṇa nijagādārthavadvacaḥ  BndP 
yatra sthitvā tu daityendraistrailokyaṃ śāsitaṃ purā 
tadgatvā śoṇitapuraṃ kuruṣva tvaṃ yathāpuram  BndP 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ śilpī sa gatvātha puraṃ mahat 
cakre 'marapuraprakhyaṃ manasaivekṣaṇena tu  BndP 
athābhiṣiktaḥ śukreṇa daiteyaiśca mahābalaiḥ 
śuśabhe parayā lakṣmyā tejasā ca samanvitaḥ  BndP 
hiraṇyāya tu yaddattaṃ kirīṭaṃ brahmaṇā purā 
sajīvamavināśyaṃ ca daityendrairapi bhūṣitam 
dadhau bhṛgusutotsṛṣṭaṃ bhaṇḍo bālārkasannibham  BndP 
cāmare candrasaṃkāśe sajīve brahma nirmite 
na rogo na ca duḥkhāni saṃdadhau yanniṣevaṇāt  BndP 
tasyātapatraṃ pradadau brahmaṇaiva purā kṛtam 
yasya cchāyāniṣaṇṇāstu bādhyante nāstrakoṭibhiḥ  BndP 
dhanuśca vijayaṃ nāma śaṅkhaṃ ca ripughātinam 
anyānyapi mahārhāṇi bhūṣaṇāni pradattavān  BndP 
tasya siṃhāsanaṃ prādādakṣayyaṃ sūryasannibham 
tataḥ siṃhāsanāsīnaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
babhūvātīva tejasvī ratnamuttejitaṃ yathā  BndP 
babhūvuratha daiteyāstayāṣṭau tu mahābalāḥ 
indraśatruramitraghno vidyunmālī vibhīṣaṇaḥ 
ugrakarmogradhanvā ca vijayaśruti pāragaḥ  BndP 
sumohinī kumudinī citrāṅgī suṃdarī tathā 
catasro vanitāstasya babhūvuḥ priyadarśanāḥ  BndP 
tamasevanta kālajñā devāḥ sarve savāsavāḥ 
syandanāsturagā nāgāḥ pādātāśca sahasraśaḥ  BndP 
saṃbabhūvurmahākāyā mahānto jitakāśinaḥ 
babhūvurdānavāḥ sarve bhṛguputramatānugāḥ  BndP 
arcayanto mahādevamāsthitāḥ śivaśāsane 
babhūvurdānavāstatra putrapautradhanānvitāḥ 
gṛhegṛhe ca yajñāśca saṃbabhūvuḥ samantataḥ  BndP 
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni mīmāṃsānyāyakādayaḥ 
pravartante sma daityānāṃ bhūyaḥ pratigṛhaṃ tadā  BndP 
yathāśrameṣu mukhyeṣu munīnāṃ ca dvijanmanām 
tathā yajñeṣu daityānāṃ bubhujurhavyabhojinaḥ  BndP 
evaṃ kṛtavato 'pyasya bhaṇḍasya jitakāśinaḥ 
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi vyatītāni kṣaṇārdhavat  BndP 
vardhamānamatho daityaṃ tapasā ca balena ca 
hīyamānabalaṃ cendraṃ saṃprekṣya kamalāpatiḥ  BndP 
sasarja sahasā kāñcinmāyāṃ lokavimohinīm 
tāmuvāca tato māyāṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ  BndP 
tvaṃ hi sarvāṇi bhūtāni mohayantī nijaujasā 
vicarasva yathākāmaṃ tvāṃ na jñāsyati kaścana  BndP 
tvaṃ tu śīghramito gatvā bhaṇḍaṃ daiteyanāyakam 
mohayitvācireṇaiva viṣayānupabhokṣyase  BndP 
evaṃ labdhvā varaṃ māyā taṃ praṇamya janārdanam 
yayāce 'psaraso mukhyāḥ sahāyārthaṃ tu kāścana  BndP 
tayā saṃprārthito bhūyaḥ preṣayāmāsa kāścana 
tābhirviśvācimukhyābhiḥ sahitā sā mṛgekṣaṇā 
prayayau mānasasyāgyaṃ taṭamujjvalabhūruham  BndP 
yatra krīḍati daityendro nijanārībhiranvitaḥ 
tatra sā mṛgaśāvākṣī mūle caṃpakaśākhinaḥ 
nivāsamakarodramyaṃ gāyantī madhurasvaram  BndP 
athāgatastu daityendro balibhirbhantribhirvṛtaḥ 
śrutvā tu vīṇāninadaṃ dadarśa ca varāṅganām  BndP 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā cārusarvāṅgīṃ vidyullekhāmivāparām 
māyāmaye mahāgarte patito madanābhidhe  BndP 
athāsya mantriṇo 'bhūvantdṛdaye smaratāpi tāḥ  BndP 
tena daiteyanāthena ciraṃ saṃprarthitā satī 
taiśca saṃprarthitāstāśca pratiśūśruvurañjasā  BndP 
yāstvalabhyā mahāyajñairaśvamedhādikairapi 
tā labdhvā mohinīmukhyā nirvṛtiṃ paramāṃ yayuḥ  BndP 
visasmarustadā vedāṃstathā devamumāpatim 
vijahuste tathā yajñakriyāścānyāḥ śubhāvahāḥ  BndP 
avamānahataścāsītteṣāmapi purohitaḥ 
muhūrttamiva teṣāṃ tu yayāvabdāyutaṃ tadā  BndP 
mohiteṣvatha daityeṣu sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ 
vimuktopadravā brahmannāmodaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ  BndP 
kadācidatha devendraṃ vīkṣya siṃhāsane sthitam 
sarvadevaiḥ parivṛtaṃ nārado munirāyayau  BndP 
praṇamya muniśārdūlaṃ jvalantamiva pāvakam 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā deveśo vākyamabravīt  BndP 
bhagavansarvadharmajña parāparavidāṃ vara 
tatraiva gamanaṃ te syādyaṃ dhanyaṃ kartumicchasi  BndP 
bhaviṣyacchobhanākāraṃ tavāgamanakāraṇam 
tvadvākyāmṛtamākarṇya śravaṇānandanirbharam 
aśeṣaduḥkhānyuttīrya kṛtārthaḥ syāṃ munīśvara  BndP 
nārada uvāca
atha saṃmohito bhaṇḍo daityendro viṣṇumāyayā 
tayā vimukto lokāṃstrīndahetāgnirivāparaḥ  BndP 
adhikastava tejobhirastrairmāyābalena ca 
tasya tejo 'pahārastu kartavyo 'tibalasya tu  BndP 
vinārādhanato devyāḥ parāśaktestu vāsava 
aśakyo 'nyena tapasā kalpakoṭiśatairapi  BndP 
puraivodayataḥ śatrorārādhayata bāliśāḥ 
ārādhitā bhagavatī sā vaḥ śreyo vidhāsyati  BndP 
evaṃ saṃbodhitastena śakro devagaṇeśvaraḥ 
taṃ muniṃ pūjayāmāsa sarvadevaiḥ samanvitaḥ 
tapase kṛtasannāho yayau haimavataṃ taṭam  BndP 
tatra bhāgīrathītīre sarvartukusumojjvale 
parāśaktermahāpūjāṃ cakre 'khilasuraiḥ samam 
indraprasthamabhūnnāmrā tadādyakhilasiddhidam  BndP 
brahmātmajopadiṣṭena kurvatāṃ vidhinā parām 
devyāstu mahatīṃ pūjāṃ japadhyānaratātmanām  BndP 
ugre tapasi saṃsthānāmananyā rpitacetasām 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi daśāhāni ca saṃyayuḥ  BndP 
mohitānatha tāndṛṣṭvā bhṛguputro mahāmatiḥ 
bhaṇḍāsuraṃ samabhyetya nijagāda purohitaḥ  BndP 
tvāmevāśritya rācaindra sadā dānavasattamāḥ 
nirbhayāstriṣu lokeṣu carantīcchavihāriṇaḥ  BndP 
jātimātraṃ hi bhavato hanti sarvānsadā hariḥ 
tenaiva nirmitā māyā yayā saṃmohito bhavān  BndP 
bhavantaṃ mohitaṃ dṛṣṭvā randhrānveṣaṇa tatparaḥ 
bhavatāṃ vijayārthāya karotīndro mahattapaḥ  BndP 
yadi tuṣṭā jagaddhātrī tasyaiva vijayo bhavet 
imāṃ māyāmayīṃ tyaktvā mantribhiḥ sahito bhavān 
gatvā haimavataṃ śailaṃ pareṣāṃ vighnamācara  BndP 
evamuktastu guruṇā hitvā paryaṅkamuttamam 
mantrivṛddhānu pāhūya yathāvṛttāntamāha saḥ  BndP 
tacchrutvā nṛpatiṃ prāha śrutavarmā vimṛśya ca 
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇāṃ rājyaṃ tava śivārpitam  BndP 
tasmādapyadhikaṃ vīra gatamāsīdanekaśaḥ 
aśakyapratikāryo 'yaṃ yaḥ kālaśivacoditaḥ  BndP 
aśakyapratikāryo 'yaṃ tadabhyarcanato vinā 
kāle tu bhogaḥ karttavyo duḥkhasya ca sukhasya vā  BndP 
athāha bhīmakarmākhyo nopekṣyo 'riryathābalam 
kriyāvighne kṛte 'smābhirvijayaste bhaviṣyati  BndP 
tava yuddhe mahārāja parārthaṃ balahāriṇī 
dattā vidyā śivenaiva tasmātte vijayaḥ sadā  BndP 
anumene ca tadvākyaṃ bhaṇḍo dānavanāyakaḥ 
nirgatya sahasenābhiryayau haimavataṃ taṭam  BndP 
tapovighnakarāndṛṣṭvā dānavāñjagadaṃbikā 
alaṅghyamakarodagre mahāprākāramujjvalam  BndP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā dānavendro 'pi kimetaditi vismitaḥ 
saṃkruddho dānavāstreṇa babhañjātibalena tu  BndP 
punareva tadagre 'bhūdalaṅghyaḥ sarvadānavaiḥ 
vāyavyāstreṇa taṃ dhīro babhañja ca nanāda ca  BndP 
paunaḥ punyena tadbhasma prābhūtpunarupasthitam 
etaddṛṣṭvā tu daityendro viṣaṇmaḥ svapuraṃ yayau  BndP 
tāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā jagaddhātrīṃ dṛṣṭvā prākāramujjvalam 
bhayādvivyathire devā vimuktasakalakriyāḥ  BndP 
tānuvāca tataḥ śakro daityendro 'yamihāgataḥ 
aśakyaḥ samare yoddhumasmābhirakhilairapi  BndP 
palāyitānāmapi no gatiranyā na kutracit 
kuṇḍaṃ yojanavistāraṃ samyakkṛtvā tu śobhanam  BndP 
mahāyāgavidhānena praṇidhāya hutāśanam 
yajāmaḥ paramāṃ śāktiṃ mahāmāsairvayaṃ surāḥ  BndP 
brahmabhūtā bhaviṣyāmo bhokṣyāmo vā triviṣṭapam 
evamuktāstu te sarvedevāḥ sendrapurogamāḥ  BndP 
vidhivajjuhuvurmāṃsānyutkṛtyotkṛtya mantrataḥ 
huteṣu sarvamāṃseṣu pādeṣu ca kareṣu ca  BndP 
hotumicchatsu deveṣu kalevaramaśeṣataḥ 
prādurbabhūva paramantejaḥ puñjo hyanuttamaḥ  BndP 
tanmadhyataḥ samudabhūccakrākāramanuttamam 
tanmadhye tu mahādevīmudayārkasamaprabhām  BndP 
jagadujjīvanakarīṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmikām 
saundaryasārasīmāṃ tāmānandarasasāgarām  BndP 
japākusumasaṃkāśāṃ dāḍimīkusumāṃbarām 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ śṛṅgāraikarasālayām  BndP 
kṛpātaraṅgitāpāṅganayanālokakaumudīm 
pāśāṅkuśekṣukodaṇḍapañcabāṇalasatkarām  BndP 
tāṃ vilokya mahādevīṃ devāḥ sarve savāsavāḥ 
praṇemurmuditātmāno bhūyobhūyo 'khilātmikam  BndP 
tayā vilokitāḥ sadyaste sarve vigatajvarāḥ 
saṃpūrṇāṅgā dṛḍhatarā vajradehā mahābalāḥ 
tuṣṭuvuśca mahādevīmaṃbikāmakhilārthadām  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne lalitāprādurbhāvo nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
devā ūcuḥ
jaya devi jaganmātarjaya devi parātpare 
jaya kalyāṇanilaye jaya kāmakalātmike  BndP 
jayakāri ca vāmākṣi jaya kāmākṣi sundari 
jayākhilasurārādhye jaya kāmeśi mānade  BndP 
jaya brahmamaye devi brahmātmakarasātmike 
jaya nārāyaṇi pare nanditāśeṣaviṣṭape  BndP 
jaya śrīkaṇṭhadayite jaya śrīlaliteṃbike 
jaya śrīvijaye devi vijaya śrīsamṛddhide  BndP 
jātasya jāyamānasya iṣṭāpūrtasya hetave 
namastasyai trijagatāṃ pālayitryai parātpare  BndP 
kalāmuhūrtakāṣṭhāhar māsartuśaradātmane 
namaḥ sahasraśīrṣāyai sahasramukhalocane  BndP 
namaḥ sahasrahastābjapādapaṅkajaśobhite 
aṇoraṇutare devi mahato 'pi mahīyasi  BndP 
parātparatare mātastejastejīyasāmapi 
atalaṃ tu bhavetpādau vitalaṃ jānunī tava  BndP 
rasātalaṃ kaṭīdeśaḥ kukṣiste dharaṇī bhavet 
hṛdayaṃ tu bhuvarlokaḥ svaste mukhamudāhṛtam  BndP 
dṛśaścandrārkadahanā diśaste bāhavoṃbike 
marutastu tavocchvāsā vācaste śrutayo 'khilāḥ  BndP 
krīḍā te lokaracanā sakhā te cinmayaḥ śivaḥ 
āhāraste sadānando vāsaste hṛdaye satām  BndP 
dṛśyādṛśya svarūpāṇi rūpāṇi bhuvanāni te 
śiroruhā ghanāste tu tārakāḥ kusumāni te  BndP 
dharmādyā bāhavaste syuradharmādyāyudhāni te 
yamāśca niyamāścaiva karapādaruhāstathā  BndP 
stanau svāhāsvadhākarau lokojjīvanakārakau 
prāṇāyāmastu te nāsā rasanā te sarasvatī  BndP 
pratyāhārastvidriṃyāṇi dhyānaṃ te dhīstu sattamā 
manaste dhāraṇāśaktirhṛdayaṃ te samādhikaḥ  BndP 
mahīruhāsteṅgaruhāḥ prabhātaṃ vasanaṃ tava 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca nityaṃ ca tava vigrahaḥ  BndP 
yajñarūpā jagaddhātrī viśvarūpā ca pāvanī 
ādau yā tu dayābhūtā sasarja nikhilāḥ prajāḥ  BndP 
hṛdayasthāpi lokānāmadṛśyā mohanātmikā  BndP 
nāmarūpavibhāgaṃ ca yā karoti svalīlayā 
tānyadhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhantī teṣvasaktārthakāmadā 
namastasyai mahādevyai sarvaśaktyai namonamaḥ  BndP 
yadājñayā pravartante vahnisūryaidumārutāḥ 
pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni tasyai devyai namonamaḥ  BndP 
yā sasarjādidhātāraṃ sargādāvādibhūridam 
dadhāra svayamevaikā tasyai devyai namonamaḥ  BndP 
yathā dhṛtā tu dhariṇī yayākāśamameyayā 
yasyāmudeti savitā tasyai devyai namonamaḥ  BndP 
yatrodeti jagatkṛtsnaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati nirbharam 
yatrāntameti kāle tu tasyai devyai namonamaḥ  BndP 
namonamaste rajase bhavāyai namonamaḥ sāttvikasaṃsthitāyai 
namonamaste tamase harāyai namonamo nirguṇataḥ śivāyai  BndP 
namonamaste jagadekamātre namonamaste jagadekapitre 
namonamaste 'khilarūpatantre namonamaste 'khilayantrarūpe  BndP 
namonamo lokagurupradhāne namonamaste 'khilavāgvibhūtyai 
namo 'stu lakṣmyai jagadekatuṣṭyai namonamaḥ śāṃbhavi sarvaśaktyai  BndP 
anādimadhyāntamapāñcabhautikaṃ hyavāṅmanogamyamatarkyavaibhavam 
arūpamadvandvamadṛṣṭagocaraṃ prabhāvamagryaṃ kathamaṃba varṇaye  BndP 
prasīda viśveśvari viśvavandite prasīda vidyeśvari vedarūpiṇi 
prasīda māyāmayi mantrāvigrahe prasīda sarveśvari sarvarūpiṇi  BndP 
iti statvā mahādevīṃ devāḥ sarve savāsavāḥ 
bhūyobhūyo namaskṛtya śaraṇaṃ jagamurañjasā  BndP 
tataḥ prasannā sā devī praṇataṃ vīkṣya vāsavam 
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa varadākhiladehinām  BndP 
indra uvāca
yadi tuṣṭāsi karyāṇi varaṃ daityendra pīḍitaḥ 
durdharaṃ jīvitaṃ dehi tvāṃ gatāḥ śaraṇārthinaḥ  BndP 
śrīdevyuvāca
ahameva vinirjitya bhaṇḍaṃ daityakulodbhavam 
acirāttava dāsyāmi trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  BndP 
nirbhayā muditāḥ santu sarve devagaṇāstathā 
ye stoṣyanti ca māṃ bhaktyā stavenānena mānavāḥ  BndP 
bhājanaṃ te bhaviṣyanti dharmaśrīyaśasāṃ sadā 
vidyāvinayasaṃpannā nīrogā dīrghajīvinaḥ  BndP 
putramitrakala trāḍhyā bhavantu madanugrahāt 
iti labdhavarā devā devendro 'pi mahābalaḥ  BndP 
āmodaṃ paramaṃ jagmustāṃ vilokya muhurmuhuḥ  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne lalitāstavarājo nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
hayagrīva uvāca
etasminneva kāle tu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
ājagāmātha deveśīṃ draṣṭukāmo maharṣibhiḥ  BndP 
ājagāma tato viṣṇurārūḍho vinatāsutam 
śivo 'pi vṛṣamārūḍhaḥ samāyāto 'khileśvarīm  BndP 
devarṣayo nāradādyāḥ samājagmurmaheśvarīm 
āyayustāṃ mahādevīṃ sarve cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ  BndP 
viśvāvasuprabhṛtayo gandharvāścaiva yakṣakāḥ 
brahmaṇātha samādiṣṭo viśvakarmā viśāṃpatiḥ  BndP 
cakāra nagaraṃ divyaṃ yathāmarapuraṃ tathā 
tato bhagavatī durgā sarvamantrādhidevatā  BndP 
vidyādhidevatā śyāmā samājagmaturaṃbikām 
brāhayādyā mātaraścaiva svasvabhūtagaṇāvṛtāḥ  BndP 
siddhayo hyaṇimādyāśca yoginyaścaiva koṭiśaḥ 
bhairavāḥ kṣetrapālāśca mahāśāstā gaṇāgraṇīḥ  BndP 
mahāgaṇeśvaraḥ skando baṭuko vīrabhadrakaḥ 
āgatya te mahādevīṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ praṇatāstadā  BndP 
tatrātha nagarīṃ ramyāṃ sāṭṭaprākāratoraṇām 
gajāśvarathaśālāḍhyāṃ rājavīthivirājitām  BndP 
sāmantānāmamātyānāṃ sainikānāṃ dvijanma nām 
vetāladāsadāsīnāṃ gṛhāṇi rucirāṇi ca  BndP 
madhyaṃ rājagṛhaṃ divyaṃ dvāragopurabhūṣitam 
śālābhirbahubhiryuktaṃ sabhā bhiruṣaśobhitam  BndP 
siṃhāsanasabhāṃ caiva navaratnamayīṃ śubhām 
madhye siṃhāsanaṃ divyaṃ cintāmaṇivīnirmitam  BndP 
svayaṃ prakāśamadvandvamudayādityasaṃnibham 
vilokya cintayāmāsa brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  BndP 
yastvetatsamadhiṣṭhāya vartate bāliśo 'pivā 
purasyāsya prabhāveṇa sarvalokādhiko bhavet  BndP 
na kevalā strī rājyārhā puruṣo 'pi tayā vinā 
maṅgalācāryasaṃyuktaṃ mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇam 
anukūlāṅganāyuktamabhiṣiñcediti śrutiḥ  BndP 
vibhātīyaṃ varārohā bhūrtā śṛṅgāradevatā 
varo 'syāstriṣu lokeṣu na cānyaḥ śaṅkarādṛte  BndP 
jaḍilo muṇḍadhārī ca virūpākṣaḥ kapālabhṛt 
kalmāṣī bhasmadigdhāṅgaḥ śmaśānāsthivibhūṣaṇaḥ  BndP 
amaṅgalāspadaṃ cainaṃ varayetsā sumaṅgalā 
iti cintayamānasya brahmaṇo 'gre maheśvaraḥ  BndP 
koṭikandarpalāvaṇyayukto divya śarīravān 
divyāṃbaradharaḥ sragvī divyagandhānulepanaḥ  BndP 
kirīṭahārakeyūrakuṇḍalādyairalaṅkṛtaḥ 
prādurbabhūva purato jaganmohana rupadhṛk  BndP 
taṃ kumāramathāliṅgya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
cakre kāmeśvaraṃ nāmnā kamanīyavapurdharam  BndP 
tasyāstu paramāśakteranurūpo varastvayam 
iti niścitya tenaiva sahitāstāmathāyayuḥ  BndP 
astuvaṃste parāṃ śaktiṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛgaśāvākṣīṃ kumāro nīlalohitaḥ 
abhavanmanmathāviṣṭo vismṛtya sakalāḥ kriyāḥ  BndP 
sāpi taṃ vīkṣya tanvaṅgo mūrtiṃmantamiva smaram 
madanāviṣṭasarvāṅgī svātmarūpamamanyata 
anyonyālokanāsaktau tāvṛbhau madanāturau  BndP 
sarvabhāvaviśeṣajñau dhṛtimantau manasvinau 
parairajñātacāritrau muhūrtāsvasthacetanau  BndP 
athovāca mahādevīṃ brahmā lokaikanāyikām 
ime devāśca ṛṣayo gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ 
tvāmīśāṃ draṣṭumicchanti sapriyāṃ paramāhave  BndP 
ko vānurūpaste devi priyo dhanyatamaḥ pumān 
lokasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya bhajasva puruṣaṃ param  BndP 
rājñī bhava purasyāsya sthitā bhava varāsane 
abhiṣiktāṃ mahābhāgairdevārṣe bhirakalmaṣaiḥ  BndP 
sāmrājyacihnasaṃyuktāṃ sarvābharaṇasaṃyutām 
sapriyāmāsanagatāṃ draṣṭumicchāmahe vayam  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne madanakāmeśvaraprādurbhāvo nāma caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ devī mandasmitamukhāṃbujā 
uvāca sa tato vākyaṃ brahmaviṣṇumukhānsurān  BndP 
svatantrāhaṃ sadā devāḥ svecchācāravihāriṇī 
mamānurūpacarito bhavitā tu mama priyaḥ  BndP 
tatheti tatpratiśrutya sarverdevaiḥ pitāmahaḥ 
uvāca ca mahādevīṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ  BndP 
kālakrītā krayakrītā pitṛdattā svayaṃyutā 
nārīpuruṣayorevamudvāhastu caturvidhaḥ  BndP 
kālakrītā tu veśyā syātkrayakrītā tu dāsikā 
gandharvodvāhitā yuktā bhāryā syātpitṛdattakā  BndP 
samānadharmiṇī yuktā bhāryā pitṛvaśaṃvadā 
yadadvaitaṃ paraṃ brahma sadasadbhāvavarjitam  BndP 
cidānandātmakaṃ tasmātprakṛtiḥ samajāyata 
tvamevāsīcca tadbrahma prakṛtiḥ sā tvameva hi  BndP 
tvamevānādirakhilā kāryakāraṇarūpiṇī 
tvāmeva hi vicinvanti yoginaḥ sanakādayaḥ  BndP 
sadasatkarmarūpāṃ ca vyaktāvyakto dayātmikām 
tvāmeva hi praśaṃsaṃti pañcabrahmasvarūpiṇīm  BndP 
tvāmeva hi sṛjasyādau tvameva hyavasi kṣaṇāt 
bhajasva puruṣaṃ kañcillokānugrahakāmyayā  BndP 
iti vijñāpitā devī brahmaṇā sakalaiḥ suraiḥ 
srajamudyamya hastena cakṣepa gaganāntare  BndP 
tayotsṛṣṭā hi sā mālā śobhayantī nabhasthalam 
papāta kaṇṭhadeśe hi tadā kāmeśvarasya tu  BndP 
tato mumudire devā brahmaviṣṇupurogamāḥ 
vavṛṣuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi mandavāteritā ghanāḥ  BndP 
athovāca vidhātā tu bhagavantaṃ janārdanam 
kartavyo vidhinodvāhastvanayoḥ śivayorhare  BndP 
muhurto devasamprāpto jaganmaṅgalakārakaḥ 
tvadrūpā hi mahādevī sahajaśca bhavānapi  BndP 
dātumarhasi kalyāṇīmasmai kāmaśivāya tu 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya devadevastrivikramaḥ  BndP 
dadau tasyai vidhānena prītyā tāṃ śaṅkarāya tu 
devarṣipitṛmukhyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ devayoginām  BndP 
kalyāṇaṃ kārayāmāsa śivayorādikeśavaḥ 
upāyanāni pradaduḥ sarve brahmādayaḥ surāḥ  BndP 
dadau brahmekṣucāpaṃ tu vajrasāramanaśvaram 
tayoḥ puṣpāyudhaṃ prādādamlānaṃ hariravyayam  BndP 
nāgapāśaṃ dadau tābhyāṃ varuṇo yādasāṃpatiḥ 
aṅkuśaṃ ca dadau tābhyāṃ viśvakarmā viśāṃpatiḥ  BndP 
kirīṭamagniḥ prāyacchattāṭaṅkau candrabhāskarau 
navaratnamayīṃ bhūṣāṃ prādādratnākaraḥ svayam  BndP 
dadau surāṇāmadhipo madhupātramathākṣayam 
cintāmaṇimayīṃ mālāṃ kuberaḥ pradadau tadā  BndP 
sāmrājyasūcakaṃ chatraṃ dadau lakṣmīpatiḥ svayam 
gaṅgā ca yamunā tābhyāṃ cāmare candrabhāsvare  BndP 
aṣṭau ca vasavo rudrā ādityāścāśvinau tathā 
dikpālā marutaḥ sādhyā gandharvāḥ pramatheśvarāḥ 
svānisvānyāyudhānyasyai pradaduḥ paritoṣitāḥ  BndP 
rathāṃśca turagānnāgānmahāvegānmahābalān 
uṣṭānarogānaśvāṃstānkṣuttṛṣṇāparivarjitān 
dadurvajropamākārānsāyudhānsaparicchadān  BndP 
athābhiṣekamātenuḥ sāmrājye śivayoḥ śivam 
athākarodvimānaṃ ca nāmnā tu kusumākaram  BndP 
vidhātāmlānamālaṃ vai nityaṃ cābhedyamāyudhaiḥ 
divi bhuvyantarikṣe ca kāmagaṃ susamṛddhimat  BndP 
yadgandhaghrāṇamātreṇa bhrāntirogakṣurdhātayaḥ 
tatkṣaṇādeva naśyanti manohlādakaraṃ śubham  BndP 
tadvimānamathāropya tāvubhau divyadaṃpatī 
cāmakhyājanacchatradhvajayaṣṭimanoharam  BndP 
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgādivividhaistauryavādanaiḥ 
sevyamānā suragaṇairnirgatya nṛpamandirāt  BndP 
yayau vīthīṃ vihāreśā śobhayantī nijaujasā 
pratiharmyāgrasaṃsthābhirapsarobhiḥ sahasraśaḥ  BndP 
salājākṣatahastābhiḥ purandhrībhiśca varṣitā 
gāthābhirmaṅgalārthābhirvīṇāveṇvādinisvanaiḥ 
tuṣyantī vīvīthivīthīṣu mandamandamathāyayau  BndP 
pratigṛhyāpsa robhistu kṛtaṃ nīrājanāvidhim 
avaruhya vimānagrātpraviveśa mahāsabhām  BndP 
siṃhāsanamadhiṣṭhāya saha devena śaṃbhunā 
yadyadvāñchanti tatrasthā manasaiva mahājanāḥ 
sarvajñā sākṣipātena tattatkāmānapūrayat  BndP 
taddṛṣṭvā caritaṃ devyā brahmā loka pitāmahaḥ 
kāmākṣīti tadābhikhyāṃ dadau kāmeśvarīti ca  BndP 
vavarṣāścaryamegho 'pi pure tasmiṃstadājñayā 
mahārhāṇi ca vastūni divyānyābharaṇāni ca  BndP 
cintāmaṇiḥ kalpavṛkṣaḥ kamalā kāmadhenavaḥ 
prativeśma tatastasthuḥ puro devyājayāya te  BndP 
tāṃ sevaikarasākārāṃ vimuktānyakriyāguṇāḥ 
sarvakāmārthasaṃyuktā hṛṣyantaḥ sārvakālikam  BndP 
pitāmaho hariścaiva mahādevaśca vāsavaḥ 
anye diśāmadhīśāstu sakalā devatāgaṇāḥ  BndP 
devarṣayo nāradādyāḥ sanakādyāśca yoginaḥ 
maharṣayaśca manvādyā vaśiṣṭhādyāstapodhanāḥ  BndP 
gandharvāpsaraso yakṣā yāścānyā devajātayaḥ 
divi bhūmyantarikṣeṣu sasaṃbādhaṃ vasaṃti ye  BndP 
te sarve cāpyasaṃbādhaṃ nivasaṃti sma tatpure  BndP 
evaṃ tadvatsalā devī nānyatraityakhilājjanāt 
toṣayāmāsa satatamanurāgeṇa bhūyasā  BndP 
rājño mahati bhūrloke viduṣaḥ sakalepsitām 
rājñī dudohābhīṣṭāni sarvabhūtalavāsinām  BndP 
trilokaikamahīpāle sāṃbike kāmaśaṅkare 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi yayuḥ kṣaṇa ivāparaḥ  BndP 
tataḥ kadā cidāgatya nārado bhagavānṛṣiḥ 
praṇamya paramāṃ śaktiṃ provāca vinayānvitaḥ  BndP 
para brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaiśvari 
madasadbhāvasaṃkalpavikalpakalanātmikā  BndP 
jagadabhyudayārthāya vyaktabhāvamupāgatā 
asajjanavināśārthā sajjanābhyudayārthinī 
pravṛttistava kalyāṇi sādhūnāṃ rakṣaṇāya hi  BndP 
ayaṃ bhaṇḍo 'suro devi bādhate jagatāṃ trayam 
tvayaikayaiva jetavyo na śakyastvaparaiḥ suraiḥ  BndP 
tvatsevaikaparā devāścirakālamihoṣitāḥ 
tvadājñayā gamiṣyanti svānisvāni purāṇi tu  BndP 
amaṅgalāni śūnyāni samṛddhārthāni saṃtvataḥ 
evaṃ vijñāpitā devī nāradenākhileśvarī 
svasvavāsanivāsāya preṣayāmāsa cāmarān  BndP 
brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ śaṃbhuṃ vāsavādīndiśāṃ patīn 
yathārhaṃ pūjayitvā tu preṣayāmāsa cāṃbikā  BndP 
aparādhaṃ tatastyaktumapi saṃpreṣitāḥ surāḥ 
svasvāṃśaiḥ śivayoḥ sevāmādipitrorakurvata  BndP 
etadākhyānamāyuṣyaṃ sarvamaṅgalakāraṇam 
āvirbhāvaṃ mahādevyāstasyā rājyābhiṣecanam  BndP 
yaḥ prātarutthito vidvānbhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaḥ 
japeddhanasamṛddhaḥ syātsudhāsaṃmitavāgbhavet  BndP 
nāśubhaṃ vidyate tasya paratreha ca dhīmataḥ 
yaśaḥ prāpnoti vipulaṃ samānottamatāmapi  BndP 
acalā śrīrbhavetasya śreyaścaiva padepade 
kadācinna bhayaṃ tasya tejasvī vīryavānbhavet  BndP 
tāpatrayavihīnaśca puruṣārthaiśca pūryate 
trisaṃdhyaṃ yo japennityaṃ dhyātvā siṃhāsaneśvarīm  BndP 
ṣaṇmāsānmahatīṃ lakṣmīṃ prāpnuyājjāpakottamaḥ  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne vaivāhikotsavo nāma pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
atha sā jagatāṃ mātā lalitā parameśvarī 
trailokyakaṇṭakaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ daityaṃ jetuṃ viniryayau  BndP 
cakāra mardalākārānaṃbhorāśīṃstu sapta te 
prabhūtamarddaladhvānaiḥ pūrayāmāsuraṃbaram  BndP 
mṛdaṅgamurajāścaiva paṭaho 'tukulīṅgaṇāḥ 
selukājhallarīrāṅghāhuhukāhuṇḍukāghaṭāḥ  BndP 
ānakāḥ paṇavāścaiva gomukhāścārdhacandrikāḥ 
yavamadhyā muṣṭimadhyā marddalāḍiṇḍimā api  BndP 
jharjharāśca barītāśca iṅgyāliṅgyaprabhedajāḥ 
uddhakāścaituhuṇḍāśca niḥsāṇā barbarāḥ pare  BndP 
huṅkārā kākatuṇḍāśca vādyabhedāstathāpare 
dadhvanuḥ śaktisenābhirāhatāḥ samarodyame  BndP 
lalitāparameśānyā aṅkuśāstrānsamudgatā 
saṃpatkarī nāma devī cacāla saha śaktibhiḥ  BndP 
anekakoṭimātaṅgaturaṅgarathapaṅktibhiḥ 
sevitā taruṇādityapāṭalā saṃpadīśvarī  BndP 
mattamuddaṇḍasaṃgrāmarasikaṃ śailasannibham 
raṇakolāhalaṃ nāma sāruroha mataṅgajam  BndP 
tāmanvagā yayau senā mahatī dhorarāviṇī 
lolābhiḥ ketumālābhirullikhantī dhanādhanāt  BndP 
tasyāśca saṃpannāthāyāḥ pīnastanasusaṃkaṭaḥ 
kaṇṭako ghanasaṃnāho ruruce vakṣasisthitaḥ  BndP 
kaṃpamānā khaḍgalatā vyarucattatkare dhṛtā 
kuṭilā kālanāthasya bhṛkuṭīva bhayaṅkarā  BndP 
utpātavātasaṃpātāccalitā iva parvatāḥ 
tāmanvagā yayuḥ koṭisaṃkhyākāḥ kuñjarottamāḥ  BndP 
atha śrīlalitādevyā śrīpāśāyudhasaṃbhavā 
atitvaritavikrāntiraśvārūḍhācalatpuraḥ  BndP 
tayā saha hayaprāyaṃ sainyaṃ heṣātaraṅgitam 
vyacaratkhurakuddālavidāritamahītalam  BndP 
vanāyujāśca kāṃbojāḥ pāradāḥ siṃdhudeśajāḥ 
ṭaṅkaṇāḥ parvatīyāśca pārasīkāstathā pare  BndP 
ajāneyā ghaṭṭadharā daradāḥ kāla vandijāḥ 
vālmīkayāvanodbhūtā gāndharvāścātha ye hayāḥ  BndP 
prāgdeśajātāḥ kairātā prāntadeśodbhavāstathā 
vinītāḥ sādhuvoḍhāro veginaḥ sthiracetasaḥ  BndP 
svāmicittaviśeṣajñā mahāyuddhasahiṣṇavaḥ 
lakṣaṇairbahubhiryuktā jitakrodhā jitaśramāḥ  BndP 
pañcadhārāsu śakṣaḍhyā vinītāśca plavānvitāḥ  BndP 
phalaśuktiśriyā yuktāḥ śvetaśuktisamanvitāḥ 
devapadmaṃ devamaṇiṃ devasvastikameva ca  BndP 
atha svastikaśuktiśca gaḍuraṃ puṣpagaṇḍikām 
etāni śubhalakṣmāṇi jyarājyapradāni ca 
vahanto vātajavanā vājinastāṃ samanvayuḥ  BndP 
aparājitanāmānamatitejasvinaṃ calam 
atyantottuṅgavarṣmāṇaṃ kavikāvilasanmukham  BndP 
pārśvadvaye 'pi patitasphuratkesaramaṇḍalam 
sthūlavāladhivikṣepakṣipyamāṇapayodharam  BndP 
jaṅghākāṇḍasamunnaddhamaṇikiṅkiṇibhāsuram 
vādayantamivoccaṇḍaiḥ khuraniṣṭhurakuṭṭanaiḥ  BndP 
bhūmaṇḍalamahāvādyaṃ vijayasya samṛddhaye 
ghoṣamāṇaṃ prati muhuḥ saṃdarśitagatikramam  BndP 
ālolacāmaravyājādvahantaṃ pakṣatī iva 
bhāṇḍairmanoharairyuktaṃ ghargharījālamaṇḍitam  BndP 
eṣāṃ ghoṣasya kapaṭāddhuṅkurvatīmi vāsurān 
aśvārūḍhā mahādevī samārūḍhā hayaṃ yayau  BndP 
caturbhirvāhubhiḥ pāśamaṅkuśaṃ vetrameva ca 
hayavalgāṃ ca dadhatī bahuvikramaśobhinī  BndP 
taruṇādityasaṅkāśā jvalatkāñcītaraṅgiṇī 
sañcacāla hayārūḍhā nartayantīva vājinam  BndP 
atha śrīdaṇḍanāthāyā niryāṇapaṭahadhvaniḥ 
uddaṇḍasindhunisvānaścakāra badhiraṃ jagat  BndP 
vajrabāṇaiḥ kaṭhoraiścabhindantyaḥ kakubho daśa 
anyuddhatabhujāśmānaḥ śaktayaḥ kāściducchritāḥ  BndP 
kāścicchrīdaṇḍanāthāyāḥ senānāsīrasaṅgatāḥ 
khaḍgaṃ phalakamādāya pupluvuścaṇḍasaktayaḥ  BndP 
atyantasainyasambādhaṃ vetrasaṃtāḍanaiḥ śataiḥ 
nivārayantyo vetriṇyo vyucchalanti smaśaktayaḥ  BndP

tataḥ śrīdaṇḍanāthāyāḥ śvetacchatraṃ sahasraśaḥ 
sphuratkarāḥ pracalitāḥ śaktayaḥ kāścidādaduḥ  BndP 
iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hayagrīvāgastyasaṃvāde lalitopākhyāne sasenavijayayātrā nāma ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
daṇḍanāthāviniryāṇe saṃkhyātītaiḥ sitaprabhaiḥ 
chatrairgaganamāreje niḥsaṃkhyāśaśimaṇḍitam  BndP 
anyonyasaktairthavalacchatrairantarghanībhavat

tamālaśyāmalākārāḥ kapilāḥ krūralocanāḥ  BndP 
sahasramahiṣārūḍhāḥ praceluḥ sūkarānanāḥ 
atha śrīdaṇḍanāthā ca karicakrarathottamāt  BndP

vyaktāsyaṃ vikaṭākāraṃ viśaṅkaṭavilocanam 
daṃṣṭrākaṭakaṭatkārabadhirīkṛtadiktaṭam  BndP 
ādikūrmakaṭhorāsthi kharparapratimairnakhaiḥ 
vibantamiva bhūcakramāpātālaṃ nimajjibhiḥ  BndP 
yojanatrayamuttuṅgaṃ vagāduddhūtavāladhim

tasyāmasurasaṃhāre pravṛttāyāṃ jvalatkrudhi 
udvegaṃ bahulaṃ prāpa trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  BndP
